Local News

Aviation Saves the Nation: Awards Ceremony Yesterday 116

More than a thousand people including central representatives attended. Awards presented by General Captain Wu, who presided over the ceremony.

Central News Agency: The award ceremony of the China Aviation Association was held at Lake Society at 1 pm yesterday. Government representatives Chu Minyi, Interior Ministry representative Lu Xirong, representatives of various award-winning groups, team members Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Fang Zhicheng, and more than a thousand guests attended. General Captain Wu Tiecheng presided over the ceremony and presented the awards. It ended at 4 pm with refreshments. The details of the meeting are described below:

Venue Arrangement 117

The award ceremony venue was set up at Lake Society on Guizhou Road. A memorial archway made of cypress was erected at the entrance, decorated with colored flowers. A cloth banner was hung in the middle, which reads: "China Aviation Association Holds Aviation Saves the Nation Awards Ceremony." Party and national flags were hung on both sides, fluttering in the wind. Boy Scouts guarded the entrance. The hall downstairs was a showroom, with the walls full of photos of various aircraft purchased by the association, photographs of previous naming ceremonies, and aircraft authorization certificates. A large table was placed in the center of the room, displaying various books published by the association and news about aviation saving the nation. At one end was a silver model of a Junkers aircraft donated by Tianchu MSG Factory, encased in a glass box, exquisitely carved, which added a lot of color to the association. The venue was in the hall on the second floor, with the walls also full of slogans. Party and national flags were hung on the podium, with a portrait of the Prime Minister in the middle. Two large tables were placed on both sides of the stage, listing the gold and silver medals awarded by the government and the silver and bronze medals donated by the association. The marble ball presented by the association to General Captain Wu Tiecheng and the marble vase presented to the late Wen Hongen, the captain of the soliciting team with the best performance, were also placed on two tables, with fresh flowers in the vase to express condolences to Wen. Around the stage were plaques presented by Mayor Wu to various groups.

Attending Representatives 118

Those who attended yesterday included National Government representative Chu Minyi, Central representative Lu Xirong, and representatives of award-winning groups: Fang Zhicheng, representing Wu Yun Chu, the owner of Tianchu MSG Factory; Mao Heyuan, representing the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association; Lin Kanghou, representing the Bankers Association, etc. Award-winning team captains Pan Gongzhan, Du Yuesheng, Xu Peihuang, individual award winners Wang Xiaolai, Zhao Jinqing, Yang Xingdi, Lao Jingxiu, etc., and guests and General Captain's Office staff Li Dachao, Zhang Yuliang, etc., more than a thousand people.

Meeting Order 119

(1) All stand at attention, (2) Play music, (3) Pay the highest respect to the Party and National Flags and the Prime Minister's portrait, (4) The Chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will, (5) Chairman's report, (6) Solicitation process report, (7) Central Representative's instruction, (8) Speech, (9) Award presentation, (10) Speech, (11) Refreshments, (12) Ceremony concludes. The presidium included Wu Tiecheng, Kong Xiangxi, Wang Zhengting, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Yu Qiaqing, and Wu Tiecheng was elected as the chairman, and the meeting started at 2 pm, with the ceremony as scheduled. The chairman and central representatives delivered speeches successively, and Wang Xiaolai, the representative of the Aviation Association, reported on the association's affairs. Then General Captain Wu Tiecheng presented the awards on behalf of the association. The emcee called the names, and representatives of the award-winning groups and individuals went to the stage to receive the awards. Those who did not attend will be sent the awards by the association.

Chairman's Speech 120

Chairman Wu Tiecheng said in his speech: The China Aviation Association was established in the 22nd year of the Republic (1933). At that time, the Shanghai Aviation Saves the Nation Movement was launched, and donations were solicited with the goal of 2 million yuan to purchase aircraft and present them to the government to consolidate national defense. From the beginning to the end of last year, although the total amount obtained was only more than 1.3 million yuan, and the actual paid amount was only more than 1.1 million yuan, which was about two-thirds of the target amount, it was no easy task for Shanghai, which had not recovered its vitality after the January 28th Incident, coupled with the impact of the world economic panic. The reasons were: (1) The citizens of Shanghai, because of the lessons of the January 28th Incident, deeply understood the importance of national defense, especially the power of the air force, so they were enthusiastic about making contributions; (2) The enthusiasm and perseverance of the team leaders and members engaged in solicitation enabled them to achieve this result. Today's award ceremony has the honor of having representatives from the central government to guide us, and the Government has awarded medals, which is an honor for Shanghai and an honor for the citizens of the city.

Solicitation Process 121

Next, Wang Xiaolai, the representative of the Aviation Association, reported on the solicitation process, saying: The China Aviation Association was established on New Year's Day in the 22nd year of the Republic (1933). After a resolution by the third executive council, Mr. Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of this city, was elected as the general captain of the Shanghai solicitation team. At the same time, an office was set up at the YMCA in Baxianqiao, and leaders from all walks of life in the city were invited to serve as team leaders, totaling 227 teams. It was stipulated that each team should solicit 10,000 yuan, with 2 million yuan as the minimum. It was also stipulated that each soliciting team should report on their results six times, once every ten days, temporarily limited to two months. As of April 3rd, a total of five reports have been submitted. The first time, a total of 266,268 yuan, 5 jiao, and 6 fen; the second time, a total of 292,842 yuan and 9 jiao and 8 fen; the third time, a total of 235,231 yuan, 3 jiao, and 8 fen; the fourth time, a total of 88,645 yuan, 1 jiao, and 5 li; the fifth time, a total of 130,918 yuan, 9 jiao, and 8 fen and 6 li. The total amount of the above five items is 1,008,807 yuan, 1 fen, and 1 li, which is only half of the original amount. The deadline was extended by one month. The sixth time, a total of 386,063 yuan and 9 jiao. The combined calculation shows that there are 1,394,870 yuan, 9 jiao, 1 fen, and 1 li. However, most of this amount is a virtual recognition, and the actual payment of cash is still very small. Therefore, although the work of soliciting members was declared over at the end of May, the office continued to urge the payment of funds and collect special donations from individuals and groups. As of the end of May, the total amount of funds paid by each team and special donations from individuals and groups was 952,363 yuan, 3 jiao, and 4 fen, which has been fully transferred to the custody committee by the office. The situation of contacting various group donations is briefly described below. The Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Association, at the second performance report meeting of the office, sent representative Wang Jinwen to report that it had recognized the solicitation of 100,000 yuan for the Aviation Saves the Nation Fund. The conference heard the news and praised it. Thus, the 100,000 yuan fund for the Fresh Meat Industry Aircraft was finalized. Later, some misunderstandings occurred in a portion. After dispatching staff to explain, the representatives of the industry, Rong Fuchang, Gu Qiusheng, Ma Jingkun, etc., discussed the solution and obtained the undertaking of the sales industry. However, there were still objections from the pig industry. Later, the sales industry association proceeded independently, collecting two cents for each pig. After detailed consultations, the four township representatives of the fresh meat industry were convened on September 20 last year to discuss and decide that the 100,000 yuan Aviation Saves the Nation Fund of the fresh meat industry would allocate two-thirds of the funds for slaughter improvement to be used as the Aviation Saves the Nation Fund, with the goal of collecting 100,000 yuan. After the deadline, it will be returned to the association for handling. Thus, the long-pending 100,000 yuan Aviation Saves the Nation Fund of the fresh meat industry was settled and handed over to the Finance Bureau for collection, and two installments have been paid, totaling more than 10,000 yuan. The travel industry sent a letter at this time to solicit 200,000 yuan for the Aviation Saves the Nation Fund. At the joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees on June 21, it was passed to handle the matter according to the method proposed by the office, but the office was requested to report to the municipal government and instruct the travel industries that have not joined the association to join the association. The office immediately sent a special letter to the municipal government for review and handling. Because travel industries that have not joined the association, although consulted, did not get a practical solution, it was delayed. Zhang Yuliang and the association have repeatedly consulted and decided that the General Captain Wu Tiecheng and the chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Wang Xiaolai will specially invite the travel industry colleagues at the Bankers Association Club and discuss the collection of aviation saving donation matters. During the meeting, it was decided that the travel industry association will properly draft the methods and report to the office, which will be forwarded to the municipal government to notify the travel industry that joined the association, and then convene a plenary meeting to determine the collection date. However, since most of the travel industry is located in the public concession and the French concession, before the collection, please the municipal government contact the authorities of the two concessions. On March 13, the travel industry association was convened again to talk and decided to convene the city travel industry representative conference on April 9 to decide unanimously to collect, and determined that the collection will start on April 15, and the method is basically still as originally agreed. Unexpectedly, the concession authorities stopped it a few days after the implementation, which led to interruption. Later, the municipal government contacted the concession authorities again and sent staff to the industry to persuade and enlighten them, and finally got the sympathy of most of the travel industry and the association. The office notified the city's travel industry to continue to collect unanimously on July 28 and appointed a number of inspectors to urge and persuade the travel industry. At the same time, the travel industry association colleagues deeply believe that aviation saves the nation and is an urgent task for saving the country and survival, so they collected opinions from all parties and recruited those who are reputable and have status in the travel industry to organize a fundraising committee to respond to the office. From then on, the travel industry aviation donation gradually increased in scale and became more solid. The travel industry aircraft fund is based on this. The Nanyang Tobacco Company recognized the solicitation of 100,000 yuan for the Aviation Saves the Nation Fund at the third performance report meeting of the office on April 5 last year. Later, it was stated that this money is specifically for the training of aviation pilots. Before this matter is held, the payment will be delayed. After repeated consultations with the company, it was finally agreed to reduce the donation by 50,000 yuan. It was immediately sent to the China Aviation Association to change the original amount, and it was also approved. The company then paid the 50,000 yuan donation to the office, which was immediately transferred to the China Aviation Association Custody Committee. Other aviation saving donations such as shipping and mining are in progress.

Representatives' Speeches 122

Next, Chu Minyi, the representative of the National Government, said: I am very honored to participate in today's grand ceremony. Shanghai has achieved this result in an economic downturn, which shows that citizens have recognized the importance of national defense, and building the army and navy is time-consuming and costly, and the effectiveness of the air force is not as great, and the money and time required for construction are less. My country's national defense has always been very empty. Now, with the advocacy of the government and the efforts of the people, we can get good results. Shanghai has already achieved success, and I hope to promote it. My country has a population of 450 million, and if we are united, the development of the air force will be fast and huge, which can be predicted. Next, Lu Xirong, the representative of the Central Government, said: The efforts of the China Aviation Association to save the country through aviation are of great significance to national defense and national survival. In terms of national defense, the center of the past world war was in Europe, and the most recent future war will be in Asia. Modern countries civilization are built on the positions of aircrafts and artillery. Powerful countries invade people, while weak countries are invaded by people. Under this situation, for the sake of their own survival, they have to be prepared. Under the advocacy of Mayor Wu in Shanghai, huge sums of money were collected in a short period of time, which is very admirable. In terms of national survival, our country has been repeatedly invaded by foreigners since the Opium War, and the nation has been greatly stimulated, especially the stimulation of the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident, so they all feel the need for air defense. The donations of the association are great in material and even greater in spirit. It is a symbol of national awakening, the general motivation for national rejuvenation.

Aviation Association's Reply 123

Finally, Wang Xiaolai, the director of the China Aviation Association, said on behalf of the association: The association has been established for two years, and I am ashamed that it has not achieved any results. At today's grand ceremony, on behalf of the association, I would like to express my gratitude to the citizens and various groups for their active participation, and I also express my gratitude to the government for its encouragement and award of medals. As for the advocacy of Mayor Wu, and the results that have been obtained, I would also like to express my deep respect, and I have specially prepared a stone ball to express my gratitude. Although the association has achieved considerable results in the city in the past two years, it has not been able to promote it to the whole country, which is quite ashamed. The meaning of saving the country through aviation has been expressed a lot, so there is no need to repeat it. Now another year has passed, and the 24th year will be here soon. The association will fulfill its responsibility of saving the country through aviation. I hope that the people of the whole country will also recognize the four characters of "saving the country through aviation". After the award ceremony, Wang, on behalf of the association, presented the stone ball to Mayor Wu for remembrance.

Recent News on the Inventory of Cultural Relics from the Palace Museum 139

The inventory of cultural relics from the Beiping Palace Museum stored in Shanghai continued last week. Page 11

The Bank Preparation Committee issued certificates of prepared assets

Public Certificates Fully Circulating in the Market. Interbank Loan Rate Yesterday Was 0.35% 140

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, after the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications allocated 10 million yuan for mortgage loans to stabilize finance, all banks and money shops in Shanghai, not limited to members of the Banking and Money Shop Associations, can register with the Central Bank. After passing the review, the loan will be granted. Settlement is required every two days, except for Fridays, when it is every three days due to Sundays. The Central Bank will announce the interbank loan rate every day at 11:00 AM. The rate was 0.35% the day before, meaning that the daily interest on every 1,000 yuan was 0.35%. Yesterday it was the same.

Money Shop Foreign Exchange Loan Rate at 0.55% 141

The foreign exchange loan rate in the money shop market, which had risen to 0.60% the day before, was the highest this year. The foreign exchange loan rates opened at 8:00 AM and 12:00 PM yesterday were both 0.55%, a decrease of 0.05% compared to yesterday. According to people in the money industry, the level of foreign exchange loan rates is entirely determined by supply and demand. Foreign exchange loan rates often rise when banks settle accounts. However, the high of 0.60% is temporary. It is expected to fall back after the final settlement. As for the rate for adding water to the head of the exchange (speculation), the highest yesterday was 0.65% and the lowest was 0.40%.

Bank Preparation Committee Issues Certificates 142

In order to regulate finance, the United Bank Preparation Committee will issue certificates after evaluating the prepared assets pledged by various banks. Originally, there were three types: public treasury certificates, mortgage certificates, and public certificates. Now they have been changed to two types: public treasury certificates and public certificates, with 50% for public treasury certificates and 50% for public certificates. (1) Public treasury funds can be used as guarantee reserves for issuing banknotes by banks and for savings deposits in various banks, and can be borrowed from committee banks at full value. (2) Public certificates are issued by the user bank and circulate in the market, replacing cash. Their nature is the same as circulating securities.

Public Certificates Fully Circulate in the Market 143

The committee is also raising a loan fund to make loans. If a committee bank lacks cash, it can borrow at full value using public certificates. The location is at the committee's office. The loan period is one month, and interest is calculated daily, determined by the standing committee at any time, and announced daily as the bank preparation committee loan interest rate. The committee banks are responsible for paying the bill immediately upon sight of the public certificates. After paying, they will wait to recover the cash from the user bank. Yesterday's public certificate loan interest rate was 1.08%, that is, 0.28% daily interest on every 1,000 yuan.

Money Shop Preparation Vault Well Stocked 144

The Money Shop United Preparation Vault has two types of prepared assets: cash and property, contributed by various member money shops. The total amount is already over 30 million yuan. The regulations for prepared assets are: (1) warehouse receipts for goods that can be immediately converted into cash, (2) real estate in this city with an appraised value, (3) cash currency or cash slips, (4) silver bullion bars or silver dollars. The preparation vault issues custody receipts. The vault can also handle deposit and loan matters for the same industry. Therefore, member money shops can borrow cash from the vault, but only with the approval of the vault's executive committee.

Wen's Demeanor 147

Wen wore a gray snowflake woolen military uniform, a beige woolen hat, and leather shoes. His complexion was slightly darker than when he attended the memorial service for Wen Hongen. He had a neatly shaved head and looked energetic, simple, and dignified.

Visiting Wu for Instructions 148

Wen Chaoji (Photo by Huadong News Agency)

Wen Chaoji, former Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, rested briefly at his residence on Jin Shenfu Road at 4:05 PM, and went to Haige Road at 9:00 PM that evening to visit Mayor Wu to ask for instructions on everything.

Wen's Brief Biography 149

Wen's alias is Zhaoming, from Wenchang, Guangdong. He is 39 years old. He was originally the lieutenant general commander of the 78th Division of the Army. He followed Chairman Chiang in suppressing bandits in Jiangxi, achieving repeated meritorious service. Wen graduated from the Yunnan Military Academy, and later from the Army University. He served as a staff officer in the headquarters of the Guangdong Bandit Suppression Army, a platoon leader in the 4th Battalion of the 2nd Regiment of the 1st Route of the Guangdong Army, a company commander in the 12th Company of the 2nd Regiment of the 2nd Brigade of the East Route Bandit Suppression Army, a company commander in the 5th Company of the 2nd Battalion of the 1st Regiment of the Guangdong Guard Army, a battalion commander in the 2nd Battalion of the 1st Regiment of the 1st Independent Division of the Revolutionary Army, a battalion commander in the 2nd Battalion of the 49th Regiment of the 17th Division of the National Revolutionary Army, a lieutenant colonel battalion commander in the 51st Battalion, a regimental commander in the 50th Regiment, a regimental commander in the 2nd Regiment of the 31st Division, a major general chief of staff in the headquarters of the 14th Army, and a major general chief of staff of the 83rd Division. On February 1, 1934, he was promoted to commander of the 78th Division. This time, the Central Government appointed him as the Chief of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and it is believed that he will implement a new policy.

Business and Industrial Circles Unite to Donate Widely 150

Extremely High Amount of Contributions Collected, Achieving Excellent Results

The general donation association is handling various general donation drives with excellent results, as detailed in various newspapers. Various trade unions in the business community are very enthusiastic about soliciting general donations. The amount of contributions received recently has been very encouraging. It is reported that the Egg Industry Trade Union submitted 100 yuan to the association yesterday. The Silk Edge Industry Trade Union also submitted 100 yuan, which was collected from the following nine companies: Huajianghao 15 yuan, Lunhuataihao 30 yuan, Tianfuhao 15 yuan, Yaoyifenghao 10 yuan, Dongqingjihao 10 yuan, Chunhuahao 5 yuan, Shengdahao 5 yuan, Yang Taixinghao 5 yuan, and Tianlunhao 5 yuan. They first submitted 100 yuan, and will continue to solicit donations from other companies for submission. The Firecracker Industry Union submitted 20 yuan.

Various factories have been withholding donations from workers for submission to the Shanghai Bank for collection. The amounts have been very high recently. Yesterday, the Hongzhang Textile Dyeing Factory donated 300 yuan, the Renfeng Factory Issuing Office 19 yuan and 66 cents, the Renfeng Factory 25 yuan and 51 cents, the Guoliang Canvas Factory 10 yuan, the Renfeng Factory Weaving Department 93 yuan and 23 cents, and the Renfeng Factory Dyeing Department 160 yuan and 87 cents. Furthermore, the general donation association, in order to conclude the work as soon as possible, is actively carrying out various general donation drives. A few factories have not yet withheld and submitted workers' donations. Yesterday, personnel were sent to various factories to discuss the matter, requesting them to fulfill their obligations as soon as possible.

Ministry of Finance Regulations for Domestic Transportation of Cash 152

In the capital and Shanghai, guarantees are provided by chambers of commerce, etc.

In other places, the customs superintendent will verify and issue the documents

The Ministry of Finance instructed the customs superintendents' offices, the chambers of commerce of Nanjing and Shanghai, and the banking and money industry associations, stating: "It has been practiced for many years that a passport must be obtained from this ministry for transporting cash. Recently, in order to prevent the smuggling of cash out of the country, all customs offices have been instructed to verify and release goods based on the passport, and no private transportation is allowed without a passport. However, the silver standard currency should still be freely circulated domestically. Now, at the time of the entry of local products into the market, transportation to and from should be facilitated. The regulations for obtaining a passport are as follows: 1. When banking and money industry firms and ordinary businesses in the capital and Shanghai regions apply for a passport for transporting cash, they should still apply to this ministry, but banks must attach a guarantee from the banking association, money shops must attach a guarantee from the money industry association, and businesses must attach a guarantee from the municipal chamber of commerce. Foreign banks should have the Central Bank forward the application for verification and issuance. 2. In other places outside the capital and Shanghai regions, the customs superintendent is allowed to pre-receive blank cash transportation passports from the ministry for immediate verification and issuance, specifying the destination and quantity to be transported, and report to the ministry for verification. After the original passport is used up, it should be submitted to the ministry for verification and cancellation. All passport fees and stamp duties on the passport should still be handled according to regulations. 3. When banking and money industry firms and ordinary businesses apply for a cash transportation passport from the nearby customs superintendent, they must have a guarantee from the local chamber of commerce or banking and money industry association. The customs superintendent should verify and issue the passport if it is clear. If there is collusion and this passport is used to smuggle goods out of the country, once verified, the superintendent will be removed and punished, and the passport-receiving firms and guaranteeing agencies will be punished according to the regulations for smuggling goods out of the country. 4. If the amount of silver coins transported in places without customs is more than 1,000 yuan, a certificate should be issued by the local chamber of commerce or banking and money industry association to be presented to the customs checkpoints and military police along the way for inspection. 5. All guarantees should guarantee that the transportation is for legitimate domestic business purposes and that there is no smuggling of goods out of the country. Otherwise, joint and several liability will be borne. The certificate should certify the transportation quantity, location, and actual purpose, and that there is no smuggling of goods out of the country. Otherwise, joint and several liability will be borne. The above five items are a flexible modification of the current regulations to ensure that laws, regulations, business conditions, and all aspects are taken into account. It will be implemented on a trial basis from today. In addition to separate consultations, this order is hereby issued to the association to forward it to all businesses for compliance."

And Ordered the Board of Directors to Report on the Past Years

Jiande Bank on North Henan Road in this port, due to financial difficulties, announced a temporary suspension of business for five days on the 8th of this month to convene a board of directors to discuss a resumption plan. Although the general manager contacted related parties to add capital, it did not materialize due to various reasons. Subsequently, the board of directors convened a shareholders' meeting, which then decided to resume business or liquidate. At 2:00 PM yesterday, a shareholders' meeting was convened at the Lixin Accountants' Office at No. 190 Ningbo Road. More than 50 shareholders, including Zhou Weinan, Liu Yaoji, and Hunji, attended. Wang Chengdian was elected as the temporary chairman. On behalf of the board of directors, accountant Pan Xulun and lawyer Qu Yue attended to report that business had been poor recently and financial turnover was not smooth, so they had no choice but to temporarily suspend business. They asked the shareholders to decide whether to resume business or liquidate. After a thorough discussion among the shareholders present, it was decided to officially declare the suspension of business and liquidate. Liu Yaoting, Zhou Weinan, Sun Lianfang, Wang Chengdian, and Wang Jinqing were elected on the spot as representatives to assist accountant Pan in organizing internal affairs and liquidation matters. However, no directors attended the meeting, and the shareholders raised questions and criticized them. How were the income and expenditure accounts, and was the share capital fully paid up? All of this had to be proven by the directors. Therefore, it has been decided that the shareholders' meeting will notify the board of directors to convene a meeting and request the board of directors to report on the past years. If they refuse to attend again at that time, legal procedures will be taken to clarify the truth.

Yesterday's Meeting of All Creditors of the China Industrial Bank 157

Passed a Resolution to Authorize Representatives to Negotiate a Settlement

Since the China Industrial Bank collapsed over a month ago, there has been no proper solution. On the 16th of this month, lawyers such as Shan Dongyu convened a meeting of all creditors. At the meeting, Luo Jiaheng, Dong Yu, Zhu Yakui, Wu Peng, Qian Zunmin, Wang Shou'an, Tang Mingshi, Yao Jiaqi, Yuan Jiliang and nine others were appointed as temporary representatives to discuss settlement methods with representatives from Lu Xihou's side. After several discussions, three methods were decided: (1) Lu Xihou would first repay half of the debts to the creditors within the year, and he would be responsible for liquidating and repaying the remaining half; (2) The debtors would request the release of Lu Xihou on bail, and the creditors could agree to this. In order to make all creditors aware of the progress of the negotiations, the representatives held a second meeting of all creditors at 2:00 PM yesterday at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce auditorium. Over a thousand creditors attended. Yin Shou Xian, Qian Zunmin, and Luo Jiaheng were elected as the presidium. Chairman Qian Zunmin first reported on the purpose of the meeting, followed by Dong Yu, the previous representative, who reported on the negotiations with the debtor's side. Next, the settlement conditions negotiated by the nine representatives and the debtor's side were discussed, and a resolution was passed on the spot. All creditors authorized the nine representatives to handle the matter. The meeting adjourned at around 4:00 PM.

It is expected that he will make great contributions when he returns to China to develop the industry. At present, I (i.e., Zhao himself) and Mr. Song Yaoqing, the general manager of the company, have decided to work hard to promote domestic goods and aim to achieve the National Government's conscience-based national salvation goals. We will not give up until we achieve this goal.

Page 12

Attached Civil Suit in the Case of Yang Jianping and Liu Shufan Also Judged Yesterday

Zhao Baoshan Should Compensate More Than 139,800 Yuan 168

The former and current directors of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation, Yang Jianping and Liu Shufan, wanted to transfer the savings of depositors to be used as capital for the bureau to engage in real estate. Zhao Baoshan, the brother of Zhao Minzhi, manager of the Shanghai Savings and Remittance Branch, was a land broker in Shanghai. Yang had a brother-in-law relationship with Zhao, so he told him about the land purchase, allowing Zhao to profit from the opportunity to sell real estate. In the autumn of the previous year, the bureau purchased two batches of land through Zhao Baoshan, who colluded with Yang Jianping to inflate the land prices and illegally profited more than 130,000 yuan, which they shared. Later, Yang and Zhao were relieved of their duties as branch managers. Ren Sijian replaced them, and he also擅自挪用储金,代逊记经营公债,使该分局受利息之损失，使 the branch suffered interest losses by擅自挪用储金,代逊记经营公债，营私舞弊，致國庫大受損失. This summer, the case was discovered, and the First Special District Court Prosecutor's Office investigated and prosecuted it according to law. After the first instance judgment, the defendants and the prosecutor both expressed dissatisfaction and appealed to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The prosecutor filed an incidental civil suit, requesting a judgment ordering compensation, because the actions of these private and fraudulent people had caused great losses to the national treasury. The Second Branch of the High Court announced its judgment on the criminal part a few days ago. Zhao Baoshan, as a public official, indirectly sought benefits for matters under his jurisdiction and was sentenced to two years of imprisonment and fined 3,000 yuan. Ren Sida's appeal was rejected, and he was sentenced to one year of imprisonment as in the first instance. The prosecutor's appeal on the criminal matter was also rejected. As for the incidental civil suit filed by the prosecutor, after presiding Judge Yu, along with Assessors Zhao Zhengtang and Zhou Han, concluded their deliberations, they determined that the losses suffered by the Savings and Remittance Bureau should be compensated by Zhao Baoshan and Ren Sida. Yesterday afternoon, presiding Judge Yu still held a hearing with Assessors Zhao and Zhou to announce the judgment. The main text of the judgment was: Ren Sida should compensate the plaintiff 186.059 yuan and interest calculated at 5% per annum from December 3, 1931 until the date of execution. Zhao Baoshan should compensate the plaintiff 139,860.14 yuan and interest calculated at 5% per annum from July 14, 1932 until the date of execution. The plaintiff's other claims were dismissed.

A Worker Dies Tragically While Watching Airplanes 169

Lost in Thought and Unaware of Being in the Road

Truck Hits, Blood Spatters Everywhere, Death is Tragic

At 2:00 PM yesterday, while airplanes were performing high-altitude techniques, a worker wearing blue cloth shirt and pants, about twenty or thirty years old, was staring intently at the airplane performance from the side of the race course on Nanjing Road. He became so lost in thought that he forgot about the traffic in the road and was hit in the waist by a truck transporting goods from a certain company. The wheels ran over his body, and blood splattered on the ground, a tragic sight. Nearby police officers saw this and immediately detained the truck and took it to the police station for questioning. They sent the body to the mortuary for examination, pending a court examination, and also to find the family of the deceased.

All employees are extremely indignant and request that the company be stopped from showing the movie. This is verified by the following factors：（一）站長與司機合夥公然販運毒品、（四大箱三大包）（二）是項毒品、公然運入貨色車、（三）站長室公然受賄、（四）站長用種種方式、誘姦生火之妻、（五）站長於逃亡後、公然殺人、（六）全部以徐家滙站及上海機廠爲背景、（七）有本路機車三只、爲C十五·十六兩號·餘一只不明、（八）有滬杭甬綫三四等車廂、（九）站長之帽章與本路警務署之飛輸帽章相同、（十）顚倒鐵路組織、爲外人所恥. Based on this, it has been verified that the content of the film is illegal and criminal, and it includes the machine factory station engine and carriages and cap badges of the railway. There is an unmistakable insult and damage to the reputation of the railway and the insult of the employees of the two roads. The evidence is obvious and cannot be covered up. In addition, the telegram from the Shanghai Machine Factory Branch has also been submitted, and a copy of the original telegram is on file. Now, all employees of the two railways are filled with indignation, and public opinion is激昂. This office believes that the matter is of great importance and should be submitted to your associations (bureaus) for urgent disposition, and a telegram should be sent to the central government for strict prohibition in order to maintain the reputation of the railway and quell public sentiment.

High Skill, Accumulation of Theft, Able to Climb Walls and Turn Over Houses 171

The Value of the Stolen Goods Reaches Over 10,000 Yuan, Finally Apprehended at Kunshan Railway Station After Repeated Investigation, The Circumstances are Complex and the Investigation Takes Time, Re-examine After Extension ｜

The habitual thief, Wang Zhaorong, also known as Wang Tianling, is 23 years old and from Huzhou. He makes a living by performing solo plays. When business is slow, he uses theft as his side business, specializing in stealing property from wealthy Chinese and Western households in the British and French Concessions. He has committed dozens of cases, and the value of the stolen goods reaches over 10,000 yuan. In the last month, two major cases occurred in the French Concession. After the victims reported to the police, Detective Liu Jinrong was sent to investigate. The thief's skills are extremely high. He can climb walls and turn over houses without leaving any traces outside. After the detective carefully studied the thief's whereabouts, he obtained fingerprints and footprints in the house, took photos, and compared them at the police station. It was confirmed to be Wang's fingerprints. Wang was punished for committing a crime in the British Concession five years ago. A cloth bag and a chisel were found in the victim's house, which were left by Wang. There was a piece of paper in the bag, on which was written Zhang Huiqing, No. 16 Xingye Li, Huayi Street. The detectives then began to investigate and arrest Wang. They inquired with Zhang about Wang's address. According to him, Wang was staying at the Dahua Hotel in Yuqing Li, Xixin Bridge Street, and gave a communication address when he met, but did not know the exact location of his home. The detectives then investigated at the Dahua Hotel. According to the bellboy, Wang often came to open a room and stay, and had many friends. The detectives waited at the hotel for three days and nights. The day before, Wu Gensheng came to the Dahua Hotel to visit Wang. The detectives asked Wu about Wang's address. Wu said that he believed Wang lived at No. 17, Huangjia Road, Xiaonanmen, Nanshi. The detectives immediately coordinated with the local Public Security Bureau to send detectives to arrest him at the address. However, only Wang's old mother was at home. When asked, she replied that her son, Wang Zhaorong, had gone to Kunshan Jiaozhi Town to perform. The detectives reported to the police chief and requested the Second Special Court to prepare a document. The detectives, accompanied by Wu Gensheng, took a car to the Kunshan County Government and requested assistance in the arrest. The county government ordered the Public Security Bureau to send detectives to Jiaozhi to arrest Wang. Unexpectedly, Wang's mother had already gone to Kunshan with a real letter to her son, instructing him to escape immediately. The detectives had already arrived and hired a motorboat to chase after him. They finally arrested Wang at the Kunshan Railway Station, took him to the county government for questioning, and then transferred him to Shanghai, where he was taken to the French Police Station. Under questioning, Wang confessed that he had sold the stolen goods to Cai Haizhong at No. 80 Zhaojiawan in the Chinese area. The detectives then arrested Cai and detained him. Yesterday, he was sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court, where Judge Wang Gangxu interrogated him. Attorney Yuan Jiahong of the police station stated the case, saying that the defendant had committed many crimes, and the circumstances were complicated and the investigation would take time, requesting that the hearing be postponed for two weeks so that a detailed investigation could be carried out before prosecuting. Then, Detective Liu Jinrong reported on the circumstances of the arrest of the defendant. Wang Zhaorong confessed that he had committed continuous theft in more than 20 households, but on July 24, he was arrested by the Public Security Bureau, sent to the court for interrogation, and released after one month. All the stolen goods were confiscated by the Public Security Bureau. After I was released, I committed two more crimes in the French Concession. Cai Haizhong admitted to receiving the stolen goods. After verifying the confessions in court, the judge ordered that the matter be re-examined on January 11, 1935, after the circumstances have been clarified. The defendants were taken back into custody.

Yongan Bank Director Accused of Fraudulent Acquisition of Property 172

Owes Delong Tobacco Company Over 50,000 Yuan Court Approves Warrant for the Arrest of Deng Jinghuan

Yongan Bank was established in a newly built massive building north of North Sichuan Road, with a claimed capital of one million yuan. Deng Jinghuan was appointed as Chairman, Ou Jiancheng as General Manager, and Ye Hancheng, Qian Youju, etc., as Directors. It began operations in September of this year, but its actual paid-up capital was only over 200,000 yuan despite the claimed million. Due to rapid expansion and numerous business lines, it suddenly announced liquidation in the newspaper on the 12th of this month due to temporary financial difficulties. Initially, it tried to resume operations, but ultimately went bankrupt due to various problems, severely impacting depositors and business partners. Delong Tobacco Company, located at the intersection of North Henan Road and Laobazi Road, is also one of the creditors, having had a deposit of 50,875 yuan wiped out by the bank's collapse. Considering that the bank went bankrupt in less than three months after opening, indicating fraudulent behavior, Wang Weiguan, the manager of Delong Tobacco Company, hired a lawyer to file a criminal lawsuit with the First Special Court, accusing Deng Jinghuan, Chairman of Yongan Bank, and Directors Ye Hancheng and Qian Youju, of fraudulent acquisition of property, along with an attached civil suit. The main points of the lawsuit stated that the defendants were the Chairman and Directors of Yongan Bank, which opened on September 8th of this year with a capital of two million yuan. The plaintiff was one of the victims, having deposited 50,875 yuan in cash, not including other ongoing deposits. They held a promissory note from the bank, dated the 11th of this month. The bank went bankrupt only three months after opening. Subsequently, the two defendants, Ye and Qian, came to negotiate, requesting a two-day extension for payment, claiming that only over 200,000 yuan of capital had been received. Recently, they saw an advertisement by lawyers representing Deng Jinghuan, attempting to blame the fleeing General Manager Ou Jiancheng alone, without any solution for the fraudulently obtained deposits, constituting the crime of fraudulent acquisition of property under Article 363 of the Criminal Code, and attached a civil suit, requesting compensation of 50,875 yuan, etc. Yesterday afternoon, this case was heard by Judge Huang Risheng at the Fifth Criminal Court. The defendants did not appear. The two defendants, Ye and Qian, had lawyers appear in court to state that Ye and Qian had gone to Pingjin and would return to Shanghai soon, requesting a postponement. Subsequently, the plaintiff Wang Weiguan submitted a petition explaining everything. Judge Huang ordered that the case be rescheduled for another hearing on January 7th at 2 PM, and a warrant for the arrest of Deng Jinghuan was approved.

Qian Shaoxun Still Suspected of Reactionary Activities After Surrender 173

No Evidence of Criminal Activity Found Permission Granted for Bail Pending Further Inquiry

Qian Shaoxun, a 29-year-old from Liyang and a staff member of the Shanghai Fish Market Preparatory Committee of the Ministry of Industry, located at 33 Sichuan Road, resided in the attic of No. 14 Renhua Lane, Saposai Road, in the French Concession. In September of this year, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, based on a report from informant Yu Shuhong, alleged that Qian had previously been a reactionary and was still involved in reactionary activities after his surrender. The Provincial Government then sent a document to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau, which forwarded it to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court, instructing the French Concession police to arrest Qian at his residence on the afternoon of the 14th of the same month and transfer him to the Third Branch of the Higher Court for interrogation and detention pending evidence from the Jiangsu Provincial Government and witnesses for cross-examination. However, the Provincial Government has not provided any evidence for a long time. The Fish Market Preparatory Committee submitted a petition requesting Qian Shaoxun's release on bail pending further instructions. Yesterday afternoon, Presiding Judge Guo Dechang, along with the judges and Prosecutor Zhang Zongru, opened the Third Criminal Court for interrogation. Qian Shaoxun stated that he worked at the Fish Market Preparatory Committee and had not participated in any reactionary activities, claiming he was falsely accused and had been detained for three or four months, requesting justice. Prosecutor Zhang stood up and stated that, to protect human rights, the defendant could not be detained solely based on verbal reports and requested the Presiding Judge to review the case. Judge Guo then consulted the Concession police lawyer, who stated that the Concession police had not found any evidence of the defendant's crime and requested the court to review the case. Judge Guo then ruled that the defendant Qian Shaoxun could be released on bail by a representative of the Fish Market Preparatory Committee, pending further review.

Station Chief and Police Officer Accused

Zhu Chuangqiu (aka Zhu Jianqiu), a 39-year-old from Changsha, Hunan, who owned the Family Food Store on Zhenru Taopu West Road, was detained by the local police station's household registration department for discrepancies in the reported population of the store. The store's apprentice, Gu Fulang, was detained overnight. The next day, Zhu went to the station to negotiate a replacement and was fined one yuan, after which Zhu was released on bail. Revisions to the Shanghai Municipal Council's Traffic Regulations 175

Flexible Measures for Hankou Road One-Way Traffic

The Public Works Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, to facilitate traffic within the Settlement, has revised several articles of the traffic regulations as recommended by the Traffic Committee, as follows: (1) Regarding one-way traffic on Hankou Road, except on Sundays and holidays, vehicles must travel east from 8:00 AM to 9:00 AM and from 1:00 PM to 2:00 PM daily. Vehicles must travel west from 12:00 PM to 1:00 PM and from 4:30 PM to 5:30 PM daily. However, chartered cars and rickshaws are not restricted. This article is on a trial basis. (2) Prohibited right turns: Except on Sundays and holidays, at the intersection of Nanjing Road, Xizang Road, and Jing'an Temple Road, from 8:30 AM to 9:30 AM, 12:00 PM to 12:30 PM, 1:30 PM to 2:30 PM, and 4:30 PM to 6:00 PM daily, vehicles are not allowed to turn right from Xizang Road onto Nanjing Road or Jing'an Temple Road. (3) Prohibited parking locations: A. The south side of Jing'an Temple Road, along the racetrack section, is prohibited from parking between 12:00 PM and 1:00 PM and between 4:30 PM and 6:00 PM daily. B. The west side of Henan Road, between Third and Fourth Roads, is prohibited from parking between 12:00 PM and 12:30 PM and between 1:30 PM and 2:30 PM and between 4:30 PM and 5:30 PM daily. C. The east side of Jiangxi Road, between Third and Fourth Roads, is prohibited from parking from 8:00 AM to 6:00 PM daily. The above restrictions do not apply on Sundays and holidays. (4) Regarding cargo trucks, starting from January 1, 1936, cargo trucks are only allowed to have the driver and one other person in the front. The driver's seat must be properly separated. Previously, the Silk Industry Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, and other groups and individuals requested the abolition of the one-way traffic on Hankou Road, claiming it hindered business. The Traffic Committee discussed it several times. However, according to investigations, although some shops on that road have closed down in recent years, it cannot be definitively concluded that it was due to the one-way traffic. Considering the commercial decline of various roads in the central district, Jiujiang Road may be even worse than Hankou Road. The reasons for relocation are mostly due to newly built houses with better sanitary facilities, leading people to abandon the old for the new. During the Traffic Committee's discussions, one member said that one-way traffic definitely discouraged customers from approaching and that protests should not be ignored. Another member said that the commerce on Hankou Road relied heavily on rickshaw passengers, so rickshaws could be allowed to travel in both directions at any time without restrictions. Another member said that the frequent changes in traffic direction were the greatest inconvenience, and if all roads were restricted to one-way traffic throughout the day, the benefits to businesses could be more evenly distributed. After deliberation, it was generally agreed that allowing rickshaws without restrictions would provide sufficient remedy, and it was decided to implement this on a trial basis. One member suggested that cargo trucks should have boards on both sides to prevent goods from falling, and the front seat should be limited to only the driver. After discussion, it was decided that one other person could be allowed in the front seat, and the Public Works Department would investigate and research whether side boards should be required before making a recommendation. The Police Chief reported that the department planned to test a set of electric automatic traffic control devices on Gordon Road and Edinburgh Road. These devices would cause vehicles to trigger an electric current when approaching an intersection, which would then activate the traffic lights. They have been effective in the United States and the United Kingdom, but each set would cost 10,000 yuan to install. There are currently 68 locations with traffic lights, which would be too expensive. After discussion, it was decided to postpone the plan and request the Police Chief to conduct further investigations during his trip to Europe.

Ya Guang Company's Newly Invented Quick Heating Electric Stove 177

An electric stove is lighter and easier to move compared to a coal stove or radiator, and it heats up instantly with the flip of a switch, without the need to add coal or remove ashes. It is clean and convenient, which are its advantages. However, the heat from an electric stove is limited to one corner of the room, unlike the widespread and even heat of a coal stove or radiator, which is its shortcoming. Ya Guang Manufacturing Company in this city, known for manufacturing bakelite and jade products and various electrical appliances, has recently invented a new quick-heating electric stove after much research and planning. Using scientific methods, it transmits the heat of the electric stove to the entire room with wind power. After several tests, it was found that in an average-sized room, one of these quick-heating electric stoves could raise the room temperature by more than ten degrees Celsius after fifteen minutes of use. Because the heat is transmitted to all directions using airflow, the temperature rises very evenly in all corners of the room after a short time, without any excessive cold or heat. Its efficiency is much higher than ordinary electric stoves or coal stoves. It is also lighter than the old-fashioned stoves and plated with chromium, making it beautiful and pleasing to the eye. It can be said to have the advantages of other stoves without their shortcomings. This type of quick-heating electric stove is sold at the China National Products Company and major electrical appliance stores in this city, and the price is quite low. It is said that purchases are very enthusiastic.

Truck Accident Caused by Excessive Speed While Turning 178

Seven Workers Thrown From Truck and Injured

At around 5:00 AM yesterday morning, a certain truck, heading from Xiaodongmen to Hongkou, was about to turn when it reached Jiuxing Road near the Hongkou Small Vegetable Market. Due to excessive speed, the turn was too sharp, causing the seven workers in the back of the truck to sway and fall to one side, breaking the wooden fence along the side of the truck. The seven workers were thrown from the truck and landed on the ground, suffering serious injuries. Gu Ermian, 42, was the most seriously injured and was sent to the hospital for treatment, where his life is in danger. Zhang Hexiao, 29, Ren Youlong, 42, Zhang Zhaoxing, 24, Shi Zegen, 29, Sun Ziyang, 50, and Zhou Wenqing, 29, suffered minor injuries and were bandaged before being discharged. The police recorded the truck's license plate number and reported it to the police station for investigation.

Judgment in the Hongwan Case in Tongkang Lane 179

Sentences and Fines Imposed

At around 9:00 PM on the 9th of this month, French Concession detectives Wang Rusong and Bao Dongwan, while patrolling Tongkang Lane across from the Slaughtering Company on Minthini Yin Road, found Li Sanfu (17 years old, from Tongzhou), a young man selling olives, acting suspiciously. They found six bags of red pills, totaling six thousand pills, under the olive basket. They arrested Li and Jiang Asi (31 years old, from Tongzhou), who was acting as a lookout. Based on their confessions, they raided a manufacturing facility at No. 263 Xinmin Village, Yaosheng Road, above the Baosheng Coal Store across the street, arresting Mao Changgen (26 years old, from Yangzhou) and Wang Akun (18 years old, from Jiaxing), seizing 62 pounds of red pills, approximately 114,000 pills, 58 pounds of unfinished material, and a complete set of manufacturing equipment. They also arrested Wu Liansheng (47 years old, from Ningbo), the owner of the Baosheng Coal Store, who was also the landlord. They were taken to the police station, transferred to the Second Special Court, and prosecuted according to the law. The interrogations have been previously reported and concluded. Yesterday, Judge Xiong appeared in the Fifth Criminal Court and ordered the defendants to appear in court. Li Sanfu was sentenced to six months in prison, Jiang Asi to eight months in prison, Wu Liansheng to one year and two months in prison, and fined 200 yuan, Mao Changgen to one year and six months in prison, and fined 100 yuan, and Wang Akun to eight months in prison. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the sentences at a rate of two days for one day of sentence. If the fines are converted to imprisonment, they will be converted at a rate of two yuan per day. The seized red pills and equipment will be confiscated and destroyed. After the sentencing, the defendants were transferred to the detention center pending further instructions.

The Economy is Declining Rapidly, Four Businesses Closed Yesterday 192

The Far West Motor Company, Heng Da Yuan Pharmacy, etc. are all in liquidation due to operational losses. According to the China Eastern News Agency, the city's commerce has been greatly depressed in recent years due to the impact of rural bankruptcy. It has become increasingly difficult to maintain. After the suspension of business of banks such as Wu Hua, China Industrial, and Jiande, as well as the Yong'an Silver Company, Jicheng Pharmacy also closed down the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning, four more businesses, including Daxi Motor Company, Heng Da Yuan Pharmacy, Xie Feng Electric Lighting and Woodware Store, and Di Xin Jewelry Store, were forced to close down due to operational losses that could no longer be sustained, and lawyers were engaged to announce liquidation. This is a testament to the fact that the city's commerce has actually become outwardly strong but inwardly weak, a sign of extreme depression. The details are as follows:

Daxi Motor Company 193

Daxi Motor Company, located at No. 2883 Jinshenfu Road in this city, has been open for many years. It was quite profitable at first, so a branch was established at No. 660 Niuzhuang Road. Recently, due to competition from other businesses and a sluggish business environment, combined with the economic downturn, it has become even more difficult to support, so it closed down yesterday and engaged lawyer Su Fuchou to announce liquidation. Lawyer Su issued the following announcement yesterday: "We have received a statement from Cao Yongquan and others, representatives of Daxi Motor Company, that the company is currently in a state of economic depression and poor business, and cannot be sustained. Our firm has been entrusted to handle the liquidation on their behalf, and hereby announces to all debtors that they must pay the outstanding debts in full to this firm within fourteen days for receipt, in order to clear the accounts. Otherwise, legal action will be taken. All creditors of the company are also requested to bring their claims to this firm for registration within fourteen days for liquidation and repayment. This is for your attention."

Heng Da Yuan Pharmacy 194

Heng Da Yuan Pharmacy, located in the southern part of this city, has been in business for quite some time and has a long history. However, business has declined recently, and the owner, Dai Dongmin, has been unable to manage it, so it closed down yesterday and engaged lawyer Zhou Shiying to represent and announce liquidation. The announcement stated:

"We have received a statement from Mr. Dong, the owner of Heng Da Yuan Pharmacy, that since the death of her late husband, there has been a lack of leadership, coupled with the impact of the economic downturn, resulting in declining business and inability to sustain it. She has been forced to engage lawyer Fei to declare liquidation in accordance with the law. Therefore, in addition to accepting the engagement, we hereby announce to the creditors of the pharmacy to register with this firm within fourteen days from the date of this announcement, in order to verify and apportion the repayment. The debtors are also required to clear their debts within the aforementioned period, otherwise the creditors will be deemed to have waived their claims and the debtors will be prosecuted according to law. Please do not delay. Furthermore, those who wish to take over the pharmacy's assets, inventory, and business location should contact this firm for negotiations. This is a special announcement."

Xie Feng Electric Lighting and Woodware Store 195

Xie Feng Electric Lighting and Woodware Store, located at No. 314 Avenue Joffre in this city, also closed down yesterday due to operational losses, and engaged lawyer Wang Peiyuan and accountant Wan Weijian to represent and announce liquidation and takeover. The announcement stated: "We have received a statement from Mr. Shen Wenbao, the owner of Xie Feng Electric Lighting and Woodware Store, that the store has recently suffered operational losses, and its economic turnover is not working, coupled with the urgent demands of creditors, it is really difficult to maintain. Therefore, we specially appointed the said lawyer and accountant to represent the announcement of the liquidation and the takeover. According to this, we urgently announce to all creditors to bring the debt certificates to the liquidation office for registration within fourteen days, in order to summarize the accounting. The debtors also hope to clear the arrears within fourteen days, take the receipt, and if they do not come after the deadline, the creditor will be deemed to be abandoned and the debt will be prosecuted. If there is anyone who wants to take over the business, please contact this liquidation office. This is a notice."

Di Xin Jewelry Store 196

Di Xin Jewelry Store in the Town God's Temple in this city announced its closure this morning and engaged lawyer Li Ming to represent the liquidation and takeover. According to Mr. Cai Dixi, the owner of Dixi Store, "Due to the economic downturn, the store has suffered excessive losses and cannot continue to operate. Please handle the liquidation and takeover." Creditors are requested to bring their claims to the office for registration within five days for verification. Debtors are also required to deliver the outstanding debts to this firm within the aforementioned period. If there is anyone who wishes to take over the business, please come to the office for a personal consultation. This is a special announcement as follows:

Special Publication Commemorating the Completion of the New Campus of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai High School

Preface 197

— Zheng Xigu

Today, we are delighted to see the completion of the new campus of our school. Looking back at the construction process, we owe a great deal to the support of the provincial and municipal governments, people from all walks of life, parents of students, and all teachers and students of the school. As we drink water, we remember the source, and we are filled with gratitude!

This publication narrates the relocation and reconstruction of our school, and includes photos of the new campus, compiled to inform those who have supported the development of our school. We believe this will be welcomed by all sectors of society.

However, the completion of the new campus can only be said to mark the end of a stage in material construction. As for the construction of the spiritual land, such as the enrichment of the school's content and the promotion of social improvement, it still depends on the supervision and guidance of the provincial and municipal governments and people from all walks of life, as well as the continued efforts of teachers and students in the school. Therefore, the compilation and printing of this publication is also intended to commemorate the past and encourage the future.

The Construction Process of the New Campus of Our School 198

Since the reorganization of our school in 1927, we have felt that the school site and buildings were no longer suitable, which had a significant impact on teaching, training, and administrative efficiency. Therefore, a plan for relocation and construction was drawn up, which was finally completed after seven years of active progress. The details of the process are described below:

(1) Reasons for Relocation

1. Small School Site: The junior high school department of our school is located on Shangwen Road inside Xiaoximen, with a school site of 23.149 mu. The senior high school department is located on Lujiabang Road outside Xiaonanmen, with a school site of 18.464 mu, totaling 41.613 mu. When the reorganization took place, there were only 700 to 800 students, and it was already felt to be cramped. In recent years, the number of students has increased daily, making it even more crowded, with no room to accommodate them. There is no campus for recreation or playground for sports. If we want to add buildings, there is no space. If we want to purchase more land, the price is high and it is not easy to acquire. Therefore, if we want to develop Shanghai High School, relocation is necessary.

2. Dilapidated Buildings: The junior high school buildings of our school were originally the site of the Zishan Academy, so some of the buildings have been around for 100 to 200 years. The rest were added during the Second Normal School era. Apart from one three-story classroom building, the rest, such as dormitories, libraries, and instrument rooms, are old and dilapidated. Although a large amount of money is spent on repairs every year, they still cannot meet the needs. The senior high school buildings were originally the site of the Commercial Press, built more than 30 years ago. Although they look quite imposing, they are not suitable for school use. Moreover, both school buildings lack proper auditoriums, libraries, and laboratories for gatherings and research by all teachers and students. Therefore, the construction of new school buildings is urgent.

3. Separate School Buildings: The senior and junior high school departments of our school have been located in two separate locations. Although they are not far apart and transportation is convenient, the school expenses are equivalent to those of two schools, and it is difficult for teachers and students from both departments to communicate. The school administration feels burdened, and the school spirit is also affected.

4. Noisy and Dusty Environment: Both the senior and junior high school departments of our school are located in the busy urban area, adjacent to shops and factories. There is heavy traffic, noise, and dust, making the air very unclean, which is detrimental to health and unsuitable for studying and training.

Due to these four reasons, Principal Zheng proposed relocation and reconstruction in the overall plan of the school after the reorganization in 1927, in order to lay a foundation for Shanghai High School for the next 100 years and to become a perfect high school.

(2) Progress

1. Germination Period: Autumn 1927 to Autumn 1929

After our school planned to relocate and rebuild in the autumn of 1927, on the one hand, the school was in the initial stage of reorganization, and maintaining order and making it on the right track took up all the time and energy, so there was no time to talk about development. On the other hand, this matter was of great importance, and in addition to all the teachers, students, and alumni of the school, it also needed the understanding and support of government offices and people from all walks of life.

2. Brewing Period: Autumn 1929 to Summer 1930

In the autumn of 1929, our school drafted the reasons for relocation and the relocation plan in detail, and also drafted the planning map of the new campus and the phased construction methods of the new campus, and submitted them to the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Jiangsu Education Department separately. The Provincial Government and the Education Department decided to submit them to the Jiangsu Education Funding Committee for discussion. After the Education Funding Committee formally passed the resolution and handed it over to the Education Department to carry out with this school, the relocation and reconstruction plan of our school was officially approved by the government.

3. Stagnation Period: Summer 1930 to Summer 1932

After the relocation and reconstruction of our school was approved by the Education Funding Committee, we planned to start the work. Initially, there was a dispute over the jurisdiction of the province and the city. Later, there was a water disaster and the national crisis of September 18th and January 28th, which resulted in the failure to proceed with the relocation plan for two years, which is a great regret.

4. Launch Period: Summer 1932 to Spring 1933

Since Director Zhou took charge of education in Jiangsu Province, he was determined to improve and spared no effort. Our school immediately submitted the relocation plan that had been stalled for two years for implementation, which was deeply supported. At that time, there was also a discussion about the jurisdiction of the province and the city, so the Provincial Government again submitted the reasons for relocation and the relocation plan of our school to the Executive Yuan. The Executive Yuan approved it and ordered the Provincial Government to be responsible for the implementation. Therefore, the Provincial Government and the Education Department organized the Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai High School New Campus Reconstruction Committee, and appointed one representative from the Provincial Government (entrusted by the Provincial Government to the Shanghai County Governor to represent), two section chiefs from the Provincial Education Department, Xiang Fu'an and Xue Qiaodong, the principal of this school, Zheng, and three local figures, Niu Tiansheng, Pan Gongzhan, and Wang Zhixin, as committee members, and designated the principal of this school, Zheng, as the chairman, to jointly plan and implement the relocation and reconstruction of this school. Therefore, the relocation and reconstruction plan of this school was smoothly implemented.

5. Implementation Period: Spring 1933 to Autumn 1934

Since the first meeting of the New Campus Reconstruction Committee on January 7, 1933, the relocation and reconstruction has been actively carried out. In one and a half years, the Reconstruction Committee has held ten meetings, and the Old Campus Site Valuation Committee has held one meeting. The details of the implementation are described below:

a. Obtaining Land License

Because our school wanted to bid for the old campus site and buildings and use the proceeds to purchase land for construction, the initial step was to write to the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau to issue a land license in order to start bidding. It took one year and four months from May 1932 to the end of August 1933 to officially obtain it. Initially, it took a long time to measure the school site, clean up the old field list and old grain declaration, and pay the field tax arrears for the past years before 1932. Later, due to the issue of provincial and municipal jurisdiction, the Land Bureau refused to issue it. Furthermore, the Municipal Farmers' Association and the District Farmers' Association prevented the sale of the former Xianmian Temple base. Principal Zheng contacted the Municipal Government Education Bureau and the Land Bureau dozens of times. Later, with the support of Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and Director Jin, the Municipal Government ordered the four bureaus of Land, Education, Finance, and Public Works to consult and issue the land license, and ordered the three bureaus of Land, Education, and Social Affairs to consult with this school to discuss the commemorative measures for the Xianmian Temple before the land license for the senior and junior high school departments was issued at the end of August.

b. Bidding for the Old Campus Site and Buildings

After our school obtained the land license, it followed the resolution of the New Campus Reconstruction Committee and wrote to the Xinhua Bank to bid for the old campus site and buildings on its behalf. In the early stage, the committee recommended five gentlemen, Gu Xinyi, Cao Zhenfei, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Zhixin, and Zheng Xigu, and one representative each from the Land Bureau and the Public Works Bureau, to form a valuation committee to discuss the minimum bid price for the senior and junior high school sites and buildings. The Reconstruction Committee revised the bidding rules and advertised for bids. After two months, no one responded to the bid. In fact, it was because the situation had been affected by the times in recent years, and the commercial aspect showed a bleak picture. And the school site area of our school is wider, so no one consulted. Later, Mr. Yao Mulian, Lu Bohong, Zhang Xiaoliang and other gentlemen from Shanghai Inland Real Estate Company supported the relocation and construction plan of our school, and bid for the two old campus sites with more than 436,700 yuan, and then bid for the two old campus buildings with 1,500 yuan in July 1934, so the problem of bidding for the old campus site and buildings was finally over.

c. Selecting and Circling New Campus Site

When our school planned to relocate and rebuild, it paid attention to the selection of the new campus site, and at the same time looked for it in various places near the urban area. It seemed that the area south of Shanghai was more suitable. When the first meeting of the New Campus Reconstruction Committee was held, four principles for selecting the new campus site were resolved as follows: (1) Economic land price, (2) Convenient transportation, (3) Suitable environment, (4) Area of 300 to 500 mu, and with development potential. Soon after, the members went to the countryside to inspect and selected 450 mu of base opposite the Chinese Cemetery in Caojing District as the new campus site. In April 1933, according to the Land Requisition Law, a request was submitted to the Provincial Education Department, which was forwarded to the Provincial Government, which was forwarded to the Ministry of the Interior. The Ministry of the Interior replied and approved the purchase, and attached a public notice, and the Provincial Government asked the Municipal Government to order the Land Bureau to cooperate in the purchase. The Land Bureau surveyed and drew detailed maps, investigated the names of the original owners, and registered the mu and announced it in the newspaper. At the same time, Mr. Yang Fuyuan, the municipal commissioner of Caojing District, helped to proceed. Since January 1934, the purchase has been in progress, and the price of each mu of land is 200 yuan, and the price of each mu along the Shanghai-Minhang Road is increased by 100 yuan. After two months, nine out of ten have been purchased. At the same time, there are two villages on the school site, with 40 houses and many graves, with more than 1,000 coffins. At that time, the villagers were persuaded to move, and 200 yuan was subsidized for each house. Those who moved graves were subsidized 5 yuan, 10 yuan, or 20 yuan for each coffin. Our school has always taken helping farmers improve agriculture as its mission, so the compensation for the farmers to move houses and graves is given at the most fair value, so the nearby residents all love our school.

d. Constructing New School Buildings

The construction plan for the new campus of our school was drafted in the autumn of 1928. A construction budget was drawn up separately, and architect Qi Minghe was hired to design the drawings. The Xinhua Bank was entrusted to invite tenders for construction. The successful bidder was the Shanghai Zhichangtai Construction Factory, which built a Longmen Building, a Xianmian Hall, an auditorium, four student dormitories, two cafeterias, a bank, a consumer cooperative, a hospital, a gymnasium, seven faculty and staff residences, a water tower, and a gatehouse. The total construction cost was 466,000 yuan. Later, a primary school and a factory were added, totaling 32,000 yuan. Among them, except for a few bungalows, all are steel-concrete structures. Construction started on March 15, 1934, and the foundation stone laying ceremony was held on May 19. It was originally scheduled to be completed by the end of August, but was postponed to mid-October due to the huge project, and our school also moved into the new campus at the end of that month. Attached below is a summary table of construction expenses:

(1) Estimated Expenditure 703,200 yuan School Site 110,000 yuan (approximately 450 mu)

Longmen Building Construction Fee 90,000 yuan

(Steel-concrete for office, library and classroom use)

(Steel-concrete can accommodate more than 1,200 students)
