Discount on Building Materials 10,000 yuan

Donations 80,000 yuan

6. Completion Period｜Winter 1934

Since the construction of the new campus of our school started in March 1934, the project has progressed smoothly and was completed in mid-October. All tap water, electricity, telephones, and sanitary facilities are also fully equipped. The school sent a letter to the Municipal Government requesting a police station from the Public Security Bureau, and a letter to the Postal Administration requesting a postal agency inside the campus. All aspects of life are very comfortable, and the scenery is elegant and the air is fresh, which is far from being comparable to the noisy cities. Our school moved entirely into the new campus from the 28th of that month. The relocation and construction of the school buildings, which had been planned and managed for seven years, was due to the efforts of Principal Zheng, and the concerted efforts of the provincial and municipal authorities, people from all walks of life, and teachers, students, and alumni. The completion ceremony for the new campus will be held on December 29 to celebrate the completion of the new campus.

(3) Future Plans

Although the initial construction plan of our school has been completed, there are many things to be done in the future. It is difficult to list all the things that need to be done. The following is a brief description of the two aspects of adding school buildings and running rural improvement:

1. Adding School Buildings: The construction this time is only the completion of the initial plan. In the next five years, we plan to add the following buildings:

Science Museum 80,000 yuan

Library 60,000 yuan

Swimming Pool 10,000 yuan

Female Dormitory 20,000 yuan

Faculty and Staff Dormitory 20,000 yuan

Student Extracurricular Activity Room 10,000 yuan

2. Running Rural Improvement: Our school bases education on life, and the school on society, so that all school facilities are integrated with social life, and the school becomes the center of transforming society. Therefore, we plan to try to run a rural improvement experimental area, starting with a small scope, and gradually promoting it when there are results. The experimental area will be within a radius of five miles around the school, with an area of approximately 80 square miles. The first step is to conduct various surveys in the experimental area, such as education surveys, economic surveys, and customs surveys. Next, based on the survey results, we will implement the following projects:

A. Universal Education: Universal education starts from two aspects: compulsory education and mass education. We will contact the Shanghai Municipal and County Education Bureaus to cooperate in carrying it out. We will set up primary schools in the experimental area to recruit school-age children, and set up mass schools to recruit out-of-school adults. Teachers and students of our school will take turns to teach, train, and manage all school affairs, and set up roving instructors to be responsible for guidance.

B. Improving Agriculture: We will designate 100 mu as a farm on the new site of our school, hire agricultural experts to manage it, and contact the agricultural experiment stations of National Central University and Jinling University to try out the superior seeds obtained after their experiments. We will also promote the new seeds to farmers. The farmer's supplementary school will be the place to instill agricultural knowledge. The farmer's supplementary school is attached to the farm and recruits young farmers aged 14 to 20. In addition to providing essential civic training, it also focuses on instilling agricultural knowledge and training agricultural skills, with a term of four years and 2 to 4 hours of teaching and practice time each day. The main aim is to cultivate the most efficient and healthy farmers.

C. Promoting Rural Sideline Products: In order to alleviate the decline of the rural economy, promoting rural sideline products is also an essential plan, such as raising chickens, ducks, bees, pigs, sheep, cattle, etc., and using vacant land to plant fruit trees and flowers. These are easy to organize, and the benefits are quite generous.

D. Running Credit Cooperatives: At present, the rural economy is extremely exhausted. Poor farmers often miss the farming season due to economic difficulties, so credit cooperation is an urgent plan. Our school bank plans to expand its service scope in the future and also run rural credit cooperation business. All farmers in the experimental area can borrow money from the bank. The interest rate is 1% per year, and no handling fee is charged. The procedures are very simple. Farmers only need to guarantee each other, and if the investigation confirms that there are no bad habits, the loan will be approved.

E. Running Consumer Cooperatives: For the purchase of daily necessities for farmers, this newspaper will contact farmers to form a consumer cooperative. A director will be set up, and business students from the school will take turns to serve. Consumers are all shareholders, and each share is 1 yuan. We will accept as many farmers' shares as possible. We will sell goods at a very low profit, and settle the accounts once at the end of the year. If there is a surplus, half will be distributed to the shareholders and half will be used for social welfare expenses.

F. Promoting Public Health: Our school doctor was originally set up to facilitate the treatment of diseases for teachers and students in the school. In the future, we plan to hire more doctors and assistants to treat farmers in the experimental area without charging medical fees. We will also provide medicine to the poor and pay attention to the prevention of diseases, such as vaccination and vaccination. The school doctor will be in charge of this. Students will use holidays to clean the streets and eliminate flies and other hygiene work.

G. Building Roads: For the convenience of rural transportation, our school and the villages in the experimental area must have a road of one zhang wide, which will be built jointly by teachers and students of our school and farmers. Before building the road, teachers and students of the school will publicize the meaning and importance of building the road to avoid resistance. When the economy is sufficient, coal slag or gravel will be added to the road to facilitate travel in rainy days.

H. Running the Defense Corps: The high school students of our school have been implementing military training for many years. In the future, we plan to focus on field exercises and assume the responsibility of defending the local area, in order to arouse the attention of farmers and gradually contact farmers to join the team and form a defense corps. The military instructors of our school will be responsible for training, and the students will assist in the handling of the team affairs, and the members will be half farmers and half students. In the future, students will gradually withdraw and farmers will gradually join, making it a purely farmer-organized defense corps.

Now, on the occasion of the completion of the new campus, I will briefly describe the reasons for the relocation and reconstruction of our school, as well as the progress and future plans. I hope that people from all walks of life will teach us.

Congratulations on the Completion of the New School Building of the Alma Mater 199

Magnificent new palace, indeed our alma mater! With soaring eaves, complete and beautiful. Near the Jiang village, the violent dust does not reach, from time to time there is a breeze, sending this singing and roaring. Cultivating talents, the wooden clapper teaches, outstanding talents, peach and plum are bright. Kind and gentle gentlemen, are blessed by the gods; innovate and renew, and the people will follow suit. We have just entered the school, without seeing the depths of the hall; celebrate the completion of the school building, holding the pen and smiling. The clouds and things of the four seasons, truly possess the wonders of all; rain and dew are selfless, and the sun and moon shine forever.

Respectful congratulations from the alumni of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai High School

Principal Zheng Tonghe 200

Sports News - Li Zhenzhong - A single pillar is hard to support the sky

National Prestige Defeated by West Tsinghai Pirates 209

59 Compared to 37, a Difference of 22

Accomplishments Still Not Profound, Heart Strong But Strength Insufficient

Hoping for National Prestige, Vowing to Destroy These Pirates

Without climbing high mountains, how can one know the plains? Observing the victories of the Central National Arts and Sports College basketball team over Datong and East Asia is truly like a whirlwind sweeping away fallen leaves, encountering no resistance. However, watching last night's match against the West Tsinghai Pirates, it still couldn't satisfy people. The strategy was ordinary, the accomplishments not profound. The entire team lacked coordination and failed to utilize methods, shooting and throwing haphazardly, relying entirely on individual skills. Li Zhenzhong stood out like a crane among chickens, merely putting on an individual performance. Whether attacking or defending, he was exhausted, truly embodying the saying "the capable are burdened with more work." The situation was initially very tense, but the national team consistently remained at a disadvantage. Initially, they closely followed, but ultimately suffered a complete defeat. The first half ended 24-18, and the final result was 59-37.

West Tsing Municipality Benefits Threefold 210

The Pirates are rampant in Shanghai, encountering no obstacles. The various Chinese teams in the Shanghai basketball scene are no match for them. This time, the arrival of the national team in Shanghai was expected to deliver a blow. Therefore, last night's match attracted a large crowd of spectators, eager to witness it. The West Tsing basketball hall was packed from top to bottom, and countless others were turned away. Based on location statistics, the attendance was probably around 1,000, marking the most spectacular event of this basketball season. The ticket prices of one dollar and five dimes were not considered expensive.

The Pirates Are Indeed Formidable 211

The fighting spirit of the Pirates is truly admirable. Their movements are agile, their passing skillful, their actions unpredictable and elusive. Smith's corner shots are accurate, consistently scoring cleanly without touching the rim, a sight to behold. Carlson and Shi Guiya are exceptionally fierce, penetrating every gap. The tall Lan Ying may appear clumsy, but for grabbing high balls, this person is essential. Li Zhenzhong was also unable to move freely due to the strict defense, preventing the national team from having any opportunities to shoot under the basket.

The National Team's Fatal Wound 212

The national team's unfamiliarity with the venue undoubtedly reduced their strength. However, the lack of a tight defense was the fatal wound. Wu Wenzhong and Gao Changming were considered too short, and their inability to coordinate further exposed vulnerabilities. This allowed Smith to roam freely. Li Huizhong, seeing the unfavorable situation, had to retreat to help defend the rebounds. The entire team relied on Li's抢刦(qiang jie) to attack. The Zhang brothers were at a complete loss. In short, the entire team's skills were not yet refined, and they needed to pay much more attention to strategy. Slow movements were a major weakness.

From Then On, Always Inferior 213

After the start, both sides dared not act recklessly, and the situation was extremely tense. West Tsing scored two consecutive points due to free throws. Li Zhenzhong's long-range shot was successful, accompanied by thunderous applause. Zhang Changjiang added one point due to Carlson's foul, taking a 3-2 lead. Carlson tied the score at 3-3. Zhang Changqing scored a free throw, leading again at 4-3. After that, the national team always remained inferior, only able to follow but never having another opportunity to show their strength. Smith and Shi Guiya launched a double-pronged attack, leading 7-4. The national team announced a time-out.

West Tsing Takes a Six-Point Lead 214

Gao Changming dashed forward and scored, narrowing the gap to one point, trying to break the deadlock. However, there was no opening to exploit, circling in the center of the court, unable to penetrate the restricted area. Smith plundered and scored two more goals. After 12-6, Wu Wenzhong also returned two goals, hoping to reach the summit. However, things didn't go as planned. Lan Ying and Carson scored seven points in a row, making it 19-10. Li Zhenzhong, sensing the unfavorable situation, volunteered to attack. He managed to get under the basket once and scored. A half-court shot also hit the target. The situation seemed to be turning around. Suddenly, two time-outs were called, and from then on, the score gradually widened. The first half ended 24-18, with West Tsing leading by six points.

Only Li Zhenzhong Suffered 215

At this point in the game, the outcome seemed predetermined. However, people hoped that the national team could suddenly deliver a surprise in the second half and perform a earth-shattering feat. Ultimately, the team's lineup didn't improve, and their heart was willing but their strength was insufficient. When the second half started, the Pirates remained the same, and the national team became even more sluggish, suffering more losses than gains. In the first five minutes, the score remained a six-point difference: 26-20, 28-22, 30-24. After that, it became 35-26. Li Zhenzhong refused to be outdone, attacking and defending tirelessly, but Smith continued to score corner shots, and Shi Guiya also broke free from restraints, becoming very arrogant. The score jumped to 51-28, a difference of 23 points, the largest difference in the entire game.

Unable to Turn the Tide 216

West Tsing was already in firm control of the victory. The veteran Sullivan was brought on, and the situation gradually eased. Gao Changming, Zhang Changqing, and Li Zhenzhong each scored, but the tide had already turned, and it was impossible to save the situation. The final result was 59 points for West Tsing and 37 points for the national team. Smith scored 26 points alone, and Li Zhenzhong scored 16 points. The two teams still need to meet once more. It is hoped that the national team will work hard and avenge last night's defeat.

Unexpectedly, Innis Defeated Yoyo 220

A Score of Two to One

The mediocre Innis football team suddenly showed its brilliance yesterday, defeating Yoyo by a score of 2-1. This was a West League Group A match. After a long period of rain, the Yiyuan field was muddy and slippery, making movement quite difficult. Yoyo's forwards were disorganized and sluggish, but fortunately their defense was solid and effective, conceding only one goal. Zhang Rongbiao's goalkeeping was bold and meticulous, saving countless dangerous shots, earning a lot of applause.

The Goalkeeping Was Commendable 221

Innis' coordination was wonderful, their running swift, their forwards outstanding, and their defense impeccable. The whole team was united, displaying a variety of beautiful techniques and a strong offensive. Fortunately, the new player Zhang Rongbiao did a good job of guarding the goal. Jiang Shanjing's tight defense repeatedly repelled the strong forces. The forwards were unremarkable, disorganized, and ineffective. After conceding a score of 1-2 in the first half, there were no further achievements in the second half. The performance of both sides was not as brilliant as in the first three-quarters of an hour.

The Goal Was Breached First 222

Innis kicked off and attacked first. Within three minutes, Kang Pei'er approached the city and reached the baseline of Yoyo's goal. Wang Shusen failed to stop him, and he was shot into the goal horizontally, which was extremely miraculous. Then, Innis' right winger sent in a corner kick. The forwards surrounded and shot, but failed to score. The momentum was astonishing. On the other hand, Yoyo's forwards were hesitant and unsatisfied. Sun Jinshun occasionally got the ball and broke through, reaching an undefended area. Innis' left inside quickly chased him down, and Lao Sun immediately passed the ball to the goal, but it was too far off and missed.

Saved a Penalty Kick 223

The audience witnessed Lao Sun's failure to make the pass and sighed regretfully. Unexpectedly, misfortune did not come singly. Luo Haiguang committed a foul in front of his own goal and was penalized with a penalty kick. The enemy's left inside kicked the ball, which hit the goalkeeper's body in the middle of the goal and was saved by the goalkeeper, narrowly escaping danger and rejoicing. However, Innis' momentum was extremely strong, and enemy traces were densely distributed in front of Yoyo's goal. Jiang and Wang, the two defenders, and Zhang, the goalkeeper, saved many dangerous shots.

Enemy Balls Came Like a String of Pearls 224

Lu Zhiming, who had been quiet for a long time, forced a corner kick. Although the pass was good, nothing was achieved. Yun Feng搶劫qiang jied the ball beside the enemy's feet and sent it out. Yong Sen brought it forward and penetrated deep into the enemy's territory, passing it to the front of the goal. Sun Jinshun was in an offside position and the shot was not counted. Suddenly, the rear was attacked again. Kang Pei'er passed the ball to the front, and Zhang Rongbiao left the goal and missed. The enemy's center forward headed the ball towards the empty goal, but fortunately it hit the crossbar and bounced back. Li Shengguan kicked it out. However, the enemy's arrogance was immense, and the balls shot like a string of pearls, extremely dangerous.

Still Remained at a Disadvantage 225

Luo Haiguang suddenly rescued Ah Dou from the chaotic army, hurried forward, passed it to Yong Sen, and then passed it to Wang Nanzhen again. Wang brought it forward a few steps and returned it to the front of the goal. Sun and Luo were blocked, and Lu Zhiming chased after them like a bird, shooting diagonally into the goal with a hard and beautiful kick. Before the cheers stopped, the enemy's Goner dodged Yun Fengdi and scored a goal easily, making it 2-1. Yoyo still remained at a disadvantage.

The Situation Was Relatively Relaxed 226

After the first half, the situation was relatively relaxed. Sun Jinshun's free kick from 20 yards in front of the enemy's goal was ineffective. Innis had very few opportunities to shoot due to Yoyo's tight defense, and because their kicks were inaccurate, they achieved nothing. Thompson once shot hard at the goal, but the ball bounced back from the post. Yoyo was eager to retaliate and ambitious, but because of bad luck and disorganized lineup, they repeatedly missed opportunities. Luo Haiguang once shot a side shot, but it was weak and ineffective. Lu Zhiming also shot a ball, but it also missed.

Yoyo Became Even More Sluggish 227

Later, Zhong Yongsen injured his leg and switched to winger. Lu Zhiming was assigned to inside forward. Before long, Liang Shutang was promoted to inside forward, Lu switched to inside back, and Wang Shusen replaced Liang as forward. The Chen line became even more sluggish. Rushing back and forth, neither side made any special progress, toiling in vain and accomplishing nothing. Finally, the enemy's Goner stole a chance to shoot in front of Yoyo's goal, soaring into the sky and causing the audience to be alarmed.

Education News

Zhejiang Provincial Education Department Asks Finance Department to Issue Arrears 233

Director Xu Promised to Raise and Issue 160,000 Yuan First

Zhejiang's education funding has never been sufficient. In recent years, many schools have been added, but the funding has increased very little. The budget for each school has been repeatedly tightened. Fortunately, there are special funds to guarantee, but the amount of special funds only accounts for 60% of the total education and cultural funds. Recently, the provincial treasury has been exhausted, and schools have not been able to receive the remaining funds, except for the special fund portion. In total, 65% of the funds for the months of July, August, September have not been received, and 40% of the funds for the months of October and November have not been received. The amount of funds that have not been received by counties and the provincial treasury before June is even greater. To date, the total amount of funds owed by the Finance Department to schools is more than 400,000 yuan. The amount owed to each school is at least three months and up to more than one year. Although repeated appeals have been made, there has been no effect. When the provincial government was about to close, it used a borrowed sum of one million yuan to issue arrears to all departments, including non-directly affiliated institutions of the provincial government, such as the courts. Only the education department was not considered. Therefore, the salaries of officials in each department have been issued until the end of December, while the salaries of schools have only been issued until the first half of August. The treatment is obviously very different when comparing them. Now that the semester is coming to an end, all expenses need to be paid, and the advanced funds need to be repaid. All schools are desperately short of money and have been forced to do so. All the principals and administrators of provincial schools in the province gathered in Hangzhou yesterday to petition the Education and Finance Departments. Those who arrived in Hangzhou included Xiang Dingrong of Hangzhou High School, Fang Hao of Jinhua Middle School, Liang Yihao of Quzhou Middle School, Wang Peide of Yanling Middle School, Zhang Yintong of Jiaxing Middle School, Zhou Xiang of Huzhou Middle School, Shen Jinxiang of Shaoxing Middle School, Shen Qida of Ningbo Middle School, Tang Shifang of Hangzhou Junior Middle School, Sun Jianwen of Hangzhou Girls' Middle School, Xiao Wei of Taizhou Middle School, Cheng Hao of Medical College, Lin Ben of People's Education Practical School, Chen Shimin of Sericulture School, Chen Xunci of Provincial Library, and Hu Douwen of Provincial People's Education Center, and more than 20 others. They first went to the Education Department at 3:00 PM, where they were received by Director Xu. Each representative presented their difficult situation and the purpose of the petition. Director Xu promised to do his best to forward the request to the Finance Department for supplementary funding. They then went to the Finance Department, where they were also received by Director Xu. Each representative stated their intention, and Director Xu expressed his understanding. He promised to raise and issue 160,000 yuan before the end of the year, and the remaining funds would be issued continuously. Each representative expressed their satisfaction.

Zhejiang Education Department Urges Establishment of Sports Committee 234

The Zhejiang Education Department, in order to promote national sports, previously organized a provincial sports committee and formulated a preliminary plan to promote national sports. It has been found that 43 counties, including Hangzhou County, have not followed the above plan to establish their respective county sports committees. Yesterday, a special order was issued to urge them to establish the committees within one month and to report the various measures for approval.

Ministry of Education Explains the Education Association Law and Elementary School Regulations 235

The Ministry of Education, based on the report of Li Wenwei, stated that the Jiangsu Provincial Education Association has not yet been completed and requested permission from the Provincial Party Department to establish it. The Provincial Party Department stipulates that each county's representative to the Provincial Education Association is limited to one person. According to Article 15 of the Implementing Rules of the Education Association Law, the representative of the county and city education association shall not exceed three people, which seems to allow for one to three people. What should be followed? Furthermore, Article 78, Paragraph 3, Section 1 of the Elementary School Regulations stipulates that those who have served as elementary school teachers for more than three years and are recognized by the education administrative organs as having made definite achievements may be exempted from examination and assessment. The so-called education administrative organ is organized by education administrative personnel. Those who are recognized as having made definite achievements seem to be determined based on the inspection reports of education administrative personnel, but whether education committee members are included in the administrative personnel and whether the inspection comments of education committee members are valid, etc. The following are separate instructions: (1) The representative of the county and city education association shall not exceed three people as stated in Article 15 of the Implementing Rules of the Education Association Law means that the maximum shall not exceed three people. As for the number of representatives, it shall be stipulated in the constitution by the higher-level education association in accordance with the provisions of the same article. (2) The definite proof of the education administrative organ is required for those who are recognized by the education administrative organ as having made definite achievements as stipulated in Article 78, Paragraph 3 of the Elementary School Regulations. For example, the education administrative organ gives comments on teaching, training, and other achievements based on the inspection report, and recognizes that definite achievements have been made. Let it be known immediately.

Provincial Shanghai Middle School Held New Campus Inauguration Ceremony Yesterday

Over 1,000 Representatives of the Party, Government, and Education Sectors and Guests Arrive; Director Zhou and Director Pan Personally Deliver Admonitory Speeches; Exhibition of Achievements and Social Gathering Held Simultaneously 236

Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai High School, the new school building located in Wujiagang, covering an area of 450 mu, is a model for high schools nationwide. Yesterday morning, the completion ceremony of the new school building and the 7th-anniversary celebration were held. The student military parade was originally scheduled for the afternoon, but due to the ground being wet, it could not be held. The details are recorded as follows:

Attendees 237

A total of approximately 1,500 to 1,600 people attended, including Director Zhou Fo-hai of the Jiangsu Education Department, Section Chief Xue Qiao-dong, Zhang Yuan-ruo representing Mayor Wu, Director Pan Gong-zhan of the Municipal Education Bureau, Director Wu Xing-ya of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, as well as Ou Yuan-huai, Jiang Wen-yu, Ren Meng-xian, Liao Zhen-ru, Chen Ji-cheng, Wang Zhi-hua, Xu Ze-xiang, Yao Mu-lian, Lu Bo-hong, Zhang Peng-chun, Cao Chu, Zhang Hai-cheng, Zhou Hou-shu, Peng Wei-ji, Wu Yuan-ji, Tang Zhi-cai, Teng Yang-zhi, along with faculty, alumni, guests, and students. The atmosphere was lively and prosperous.

A Glimpse 238

The school's land covers more than 450 mu, which is very large. The southwest is a sports field, the northwest is a farm, and the east is the school building. The buildings that have already been constructed include a Longmen Building, a Xianmian Hall, an auditorium, a factory, a gymnasium, an elementary school, four student dormitories, six dining halls, six kitchens, seven faculty residences, and a hospital and cooperative. The exterior is extremely solemn and grand, and the interior is even more substantial and rich. The achievements are remarkable and impressive, truly a model among secondary schools nationwide.

Ceremony Details 239

At 10:00 AM, the completion ceremony and 7th-anniversary celebration were held in the auditorium, presided over by Principal Zheng Xi-gu, with Zhang Zhong-bao and Lu Shao-ji providing hospitality. After the ceremonial rituals, Principal Zheng Xi-gu first reported on the construction process and the significance of the anniversary. Then, Director Zhou Fo-hai of the Jiangsu Education Department, Zhang Yuan-ruo representing Mayor Wu, Director Pan Gong-zhan of the Municipal Education Bureau, Director Wu Xing-ya of the Social Affairs Bureau, and guest Zhang Peng-chun delivered speeches successively. Following that, representatives of the faculty and students delivered speeches. The ceremony concluded with the playing of music, a group photograph, and adjournment.

Chairman's Report 240

Chairman Zheng Xi-gu reported, roughly stating that today the school is holding the completion ceremony and 7th-anniversary celebration. It is a great honor to have the presence of officials and guests. There are two layers of significance to today's meeting. First, the school's construction and relocation have been successfully carried out with the support of all parties, which is greatly appreciated. Second, the work of the school's teachers and students will be even greater in the future, and it will require the assistance and guidance of the government, the community, and the parents of students at all times. Since the reorganization in the 16th year of the Republic, the school has had a plan to relocate. The plan was submitted to the Provincial Government and the Education Department in the 18th year of the Republic, and it was actively carried out with the assistance of Director Zhou and the municipal authorities in the 21st year of the Republic. A committee was also organized to take charge of the matter. First, the old site was sold for 470,000 yuan. At the same time, 450 mu of land was purchased in Wujiagang for a total of 110,000 yuan, the construction of the school building cost 490,000 yuan, the equipment cost 100,000 yuan, and other expenses amounted to 20,000 yuan, totaling 730,000 yuan. The income fell short by 100,000 yuan, and fundraising is currently underway. Now that the school building has been completed, the work of the school's teachers and students will be even greater. Only by boosting spirits can they live up to the expectations of all parties.

Director Zhou's Speech 241

Director Zhou Fo-hai of the Jiangsu Education Department gave a speech, roughly stating that it is a great pleasure to participate in the completion ceremony of the new Shanghai High School building. Just now, listening to Principal Zheng's report, from the planning and sale of the old site to the completion of the new school building, countless difficulties were encountered before reaching today's goal. This is entirely due to the assistance of the municipal authorities and all parties, as well as the efforts of Principal Zheng and the faculty. Today, I, on behalf of the provincial government, express my gratitude to the Shanghai municipal authorities and all sectors of society, and offer my condolences to Principal Zheng and others. At the same time, I hope that the Shanghai municipal authorities will continue to provide assistance, and I hope that Principal Zheng and others will continue to work hard. The new Shanghai High School building can be considered one of the best in China. At the same time, I hope that the students of Shanghai High School will reach the same level of excellence in their physical fitness and academic knowledge. Chairman Chiang recently inspected various places in the Northwest and believes that various undertakings have made progress, but education has not made progress. The reason for this is the lack of physical strength. The reason for the lack of physical strength is nothing more than insufficient nutrition, overwork, or lack of exercise. I hope that the students of Shanghai High School will quickly strengthen their physical fitness. Second, they must cultivate their personality and develop the ability to adapt to the environment. Third, they must increase their knowledge. If the students can focus on these three points, then the relocation of Shanghai High School will have meaning.

Mayor Wu's Speech 242

Zhang Yuan-ruo, representing Mayor Wu, said that the new Shanghai High School building covers an area of 450 mu, and its excellent environment makes it a standard high school in China. Principal Zheng Xi-gu is a strong researcher of secondary education and can be considered a standard principal. Having a standard school and a standard principal, it is impossible not to have standard students. The importance of the status of young students is undeniable. If we want to create a strong and beautiful nation, we need to cultivate standard young students from today onwards. Today's youth must recognize the relationship between national life and cultivate future talents to carry on the past and create the driving force for the creation of national life. Youth and the nation are like white blood cells and the human body. Without white blood cells, the human body is prone to disease. Without standard youth, the nation will be in immediate danger. I hope that from today's completion of the new school building, a large number of new young people will be cultivated to build the nation.

Director Pan's Speech 243

Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau said that he just heard the speeches of Director Zhou and Mr. Zhang representing Mayor Wu, who said that to be a standard young person, one must cultivate oneself in terms of physical fitness, knowledge, and personality. I have some additional opinions to add. First, in addition to cultivating physical fitness, personality, and knowledge, young people must also have a national spirit and a spirit of the times. The national spirit is vertical, with historical connections, and the spirit of the times is horizontal, with geographical connections. Young people cultivated from these two spirits are the young people China needs. Furthermore, education should have a consistent goal. Standard students are created under the rules and norms of principals and teachers. Therefore, the issue of teachers is very important. Hu Shi recently had a theory that young people should explore on their own. Blindly groping for ten years can find a way out. He also said that if Chinese youth do not believe in Marxism at the age of twenty, they will not be successful, and if they believe in Marxism at the age of thirty, they will also not be successful. This kind of arrogant argument is beyond description. I hope that students of Shanghai High School, under the leadership of standard teachers, will never blindly follow the words of such university professors when they enter university in the future.

Director Wu's Speech 244

Director Wu Xing-ya of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau said that the gentlemen just spoke about nothing more than the cultivation of physical fitness, personality, and knowledge. At the same time, young people must have a national spirit and a spirit of the times, and it is especially important not to blindly follow the arrogant words of university professors. It is very important to accept the opinions of the gentlemen, but I believe that the most important thing is to first restore national self-confidence. Young people should not talk empty words in this era, but should start from the root. The gentlemen have already spoken in great detail. In recent years, the slogan of revitalizing the nation has permeated the country. To revitalize the Chinese nation and build a new China, this responsibility lies on the shoulders of the youth who carry on the past and open up the future.

Exhibition of Achievements 245

The school also began to publicly exhibit all its achievements from yesterday onwards. The students' usual academic achievements are displayed on the first floor of Xianmian Hall, the achievements of various rooms in physics and chemistry are displayed in the physics and chemistry experiment and equipment and medicine room, the biological achievements are displayed in the biological experiment room and specimen room, the labor achievements are displayed in the achievement room of Longmen Building, the drawing achievements are displayed in the drawing classroom, the school's administrative achievements are displayed in the conference room and reception room, and the achievements of the industrial and commercial departments are displayed in the special classroom of the industrial and commercial departments. Yesterday, the guests and parents of students who visited were in an endless stream, and today is Sunday, so it will be even more enthusiastic.

General Activities 246

The school originally scheduled to hold the anniversary celebration on the morning of the 29th and the student military and Boy Scout parade in the afternoon. Financial Gold Market Experiences Sharp Fluctuations 255

Kuan Gold Plummets, Exchange Rate Tightens, Once Reaching 60 Yuan; Rumors of Favorable News Lead to Buying Activity, Rebounding 2.7 Yuan

The market yesterday was characterized by fluctuating sentiment and extremely narrow margins. With a single change, the fluctuations were significant. Initially, the overall trend was downward due to the tightening exchange rate, with multiple parties continuously collapsing. However, in the end, due to various rumors unfavorable to the selling side, there was excitement, and the buying surge rebounded quickly. Initially, overseas silver markets in England and America rose in unison, and the forward silver price in MonteVideo rose by another six points, slightly contracting the exchange rate. The price of raw gold in London remained unchanged. When off-site preparatory trading opened, it immediately retreated to 62.3 yuan, and then retreated within 1 yuan. Major players such as Fuxing, Yongheng, and Yu made efforts to buy, gradually rebounding. The Central Bank's listing revealed that the British pound rose by 1.25 and the US dollar rose by 2.5. The customs gold unit fell by another 1.5 points, and the standard gold price retreated to 999 yuan and 20 cents, leading to a fall immediately after opening. Although the Jewish merchant Qiao Zhifu stuffed shillings first, the gradual recovery was good due to the healthy absorption of banks. Although there was a struggle because it was known that the HSBC bank would list a rise of 1.25 for the British pound and 2.5 for the US dollar, the exchange rate tightened at this time, and major players purchased in unison, rising once. However, because those who took the opportunity to sell at high prices were still active, the price gradually fell back. At this time, because the banks were still absorbing, the white silver balance tax was revealed to have risen by 2.5, calculated at 6% and the British exchange rate was calculated at 1 shilling and 5 pence and 59375, which was relatively stable. Unexpectedly, the buying absorption of HSBC and other banks suddenly stagnated, and the banks suddenly had a selling absorption, so the exchange rate reported loose and excessive. Major players took the opportunity to sell off, and the buying side panicked again, and the downward trend was formed. Although China tried to maintain it, the supply was greater than the demand, which made buyers dare not act. The price fell below the 60-yuan mark and then fell to a low price of 56.5 yuan. The price was maintained when the price was low, and the selling wind also stopped, gradually rising back to more than 60 yuan. Many parties saw an opportunity and worked hard. The table was very barren because the short position had increased too much, and floating households were unable to supply the terms. The cotton market is quite firm because Indian cotton is rising more and more, and gold prices are also slightly rising. However, the current cotton demand is extremely quiet. There are no transactions. The source of arrival is 773 bales of Yao cotton.

A Brief Record of Yarn and Cotton Delivery 262

Yarn

The December gold yarn futures were listed on July 2nd of this year. The opening price of the first session was 184.8 yuan, slightly down to 3.7 yuan. At this time, rumors about the Shenxin factory were spreading, and there were various discussions in the market, saying that the factory would completely stop work for reorganization. General speculators had delusions because the factory had a large production capacity. If it really stopped, it would have a significant impact on the market. Buyers swarmed in. At the same time, the climate in the country was extremely dry, the cotton market was firm, and the financial sector also bought a large amount to go long. The demand for coarse yarn from North China was also smooth. The market gradually trended upward, and there was once a lively scene. The highest price was around 191 yuan. Unexpectedly, the United States implemented a policy of buying silver, the price of silver rose sharply, and the price of gold trended down, causing the prices of goods in our country to appear quite unstable. The exchange rate of the Japanese yen increased to more than 127 yuan, causing Japanese merchants to sell off aggressively. The market fell further and further, and the lowest price was 170.05 yuan. Later, in October, the government, in view of the increasing outflow of silver, increased the export tax and added a balancing tax on silver to maintain the stability of Shanghai's finance, which caused the weak and sluggish yarn market to suddenly soar, and the highest price reached 188.8 yuan. Extending to the middle of this month, it hovered between 182 and 183 yuan for a long time. Later, due to a large household receiving goods, the last session jumped wildly to 187 yuan. The result of the delivery price was 180 yuan, which was 3 yuan higher than the November period. There were 5,750 bales remaining. The actual delivery was 2,300 bales of 20-count Saiyu yarn, 350 bales of Ren Zhong, 150 bales of Baoyi, and 150 bales of Shepherd. The rest were self-delivered. Wu was the largest receiver, followed by Tongcheng Company. The broker numbers and bale amounts of the receiving and delivering manufacturers and arbitrageurs are listed below (unit: bales).

▲ Seller's Delivery

Hengda 1,000, Jifeng 200, Dafu 50, Tongfu 100, Hengyi 1,450, Yukang 100, Dafeng 200, Yuanda 150, Jinchang 1,050, Mingde 250, Changji 250, Shenchang 50, Junchang 100, Tongfeng 300, Changfeng 350, Yongda 50

▲ Buyer's Receipt

Dafu 250, Tongji 450, Yuda 750, Suilong 900, Jinchang 1,050, Shenchang 350, Junchang 100, Hengde 250, Renfeng 750, Yuanyi 400, Changfeng 350, Yongda 50

Cotton

The December standard cotton futures were listed on July 2nd of this year. The opening price of the first session was 35.3 yuan, slightly down to around 4 yuan. Later, due to the dry climate in the country and the drought that had already formed, the development of new cotton was greatly affected. American cotton fields were reduced, and everyone unanimously hoped for an increase. The highest price was 37 yuan. Although the government's estimated announcement on August 8th was an increase, Wang of a yarn factory and Tongcheng Company aggressively sold off about 200,000 dan. The market was under pressure, and the market price gradually decreased from 37 yuan. Later, in the middle of October, the national cotton report estimated a bumper harvest due to a large increase in the number of people who changed to planting cotton fields because agricultural products were cheap in the previous year. Buyers were disappointed. At the same time, the yarn market did not rise, and there were many factories reducing working hours. As a result, the cotton market had a low of 33 yuan. Until the middle of October, the national government prevented the outflow of silver, increased the export tax on silver, and added a balancing tax. The price of gold rose sharply, and the prices of all goods soared. The price of cotton rose from 34 yuan straight to 38 yuan. Extending to this month, it hovered outside 36 yuan for a long time. As a result, the last session price was 36.1 yuan, which was 4.5 jiao lower than the November price. There were 18,200 dan remaining. The actual delivery was only 5,800 dan, and the rest were self-delivered. The goods included Yao cotton, Shandong coarse velvet, and Hankou group velvet. The delivery price was 36.5 yuan. The broker numbers and bale amounts of the receiving and delivering parties are listed below (unit: dan).

▲ Seller's Delivery

Hengyi 3,900, Shenchang 1,400, Changhe 1,900

▲ Buyer's Receipt

Jifeng 200, Dafu 1,900, Suilong 2,900, Tongxing 400, Yida 1,000, Yikang 800

Many Changes in Yarn and Cotton Grades for the June 24th Period 263

|Increase of One to Two Yuan for Fine Velvet Grades|

The Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Exchange held a cotton appraisal meeting on December 23rd to supply the delivery for the June 24th period. As a result of the appraisal of grade changes, the original addition of 7 yuan for Grade 1 Medium B was changed to an addition of 6 yuan, the original addition of 6 yuan for Grade C was changed to an addition of 4.5 yuan, and the original addition of 5 yuan for Grade D was changed to an addition of 3 yuan. For Grade 2, the original addition of 1 yuan for Grade A was changed to an addition of 2 yuan, the original reduction of 1.2 jiao for Grade C was changed to a reduction of 1.5 jiao, and the original reduction of 1.7 jiao for Grade B was changed to a reduction of 1.8 jiao. Grade 4 has no changes at all. The changed procedures, grades, and prices are excerpted below (for reference).

▲ Grade 1 New Price Original Price Grade A Add 10 Yuan Add 10 Yuan Grade B Add 6 Yuan Add 7 Yuan Grade C Add 4.5 Yuan Add 6 Yuan Grade D Add 3 Yuan Add 5 Yuan

▲ Grade 2

▲ Grade 3

Grade A Reduce 1.5 Yuan Reduce 1.2 Jiao Grade B Reduce 1.8 Yuan Reduce 1.7 Jiao Grade C Reduce 2.3 Jiao Grade D Reduce 2.7 Jiao

Furthermore, the Cotton Yarn Review Committee convened an appraisal meeting on December 26th to serve as a substitute for the June 24th period for delivery. As a result, the 10-count and 16-count grades had no changes and were the same as the May period. However, the original reduction of 5 yuan for the 20-count Cai Feiji brand from the Pudong Hengda Factory was raised one level and changed to a reduction of 4 yuan. However, the 20-count Fugui from the Hengfeng Factory was reduced by another level, from an original reduction of 5 yuan to a reduction of 6 yuan. There were no changes to the other yarn brands.

Slight Improvement in Overseas Cotton Market 264

Yesterday, the US cotton market opened, and the market was firm and rising. Each month rose by 4 to 10 points. Afterwards, the Liverpool and Bombay telegrams were good. Liverpool brokers, colleagues, and spot traders bought in, and the market was even better. In the middle of the session, due to the approaching New Year holiday, long positions were closed and southern sales were set, and a slight return wind was seen. However, the wheat market and stocks both rose, and were eventually driven up. The spot basis was firm, and demand was flat. The closing was tight and stable. (Hays estimate, the plant uses 216,000 bales, Liverpool storage is 289,000 bales.) The spot price rose by 10 points, and the futures price rose by 8 to 14 points. Both the British cotton futures and spot prices rose by 4 points. Indian cotton was initially firm due to short covering and buying by futures traders, but later weakened due to selling by European exporters and brokers. Pirgo rose by 3.25 rupees, Aumla rose by 5.25 rupees, and Balochi rose by 4.25 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (telegram of the 28th).

Increased Hopes for US Cotton Exports 265

A New York telegram on December 28th reported the cotton market situation for the week, stating that the cotton market was relatively quiet due to Christmas. Domestic commercial news was good, and the foreign cotton market had been firm recently, so there was some price-fixing and retail buying. However, some people set up sales and closed long positions, which led to the curtailment of the rising trend. With the New Year approaching, the future of the cotton industry is now optimistic, and the saying that foreign cotton competition is gradually decreasing has aroused hopes for increased US cotton exports. However, there are several obstacles to the increase, one of which is that the authorities' cotton production procedures for next year are still doubtful, the second is that the 12-cent loan may not have a fixed price force, and the third is that the 1.7 million bales of cotton stored by the cotton farmers' public storage agency may be gradually sold when the market price is slightly higher than the loan price. It is speculated that the authorities will take into account the general business situation and slightly increase next year's sales, and will also pay more attention to the foreign market for US cotton.

Grain, Downriver Rice Sales Sluggish, Seen Falling 266

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources for each group were relatively scarce, with only a dozen or so arriving (goods totaling nearly 3,000 shi), while the sales market was particularly sluggish due to year-end and monetary issues. Later, due to the sunny weather, people's hearts were still soft, resulting in a quiet situation and the market color suddenly turned downward. For example, the prices of each thick japonica rice returned to several fen to a jiao, while although there were customers moving in late rice, the result was only a few hundred bales handled by the Tongzhou group, which did not help the overall situation and presented the same scene. The various colors of Du Yang tip and yinbian yuan also fell by more than a chi.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, there were 34 or 35 sources from downriver and inland areas. In terms of market sales, the appetite for white japonica rice was slightly exchanged, and the retail appetite was still attractive in the morning market, but turned sluggish in the afternoon market. Early thin rice was carefully selected for high prices, yinbian yuan was normal, and Yang Du tip arrivals were slightly available, but sales were also slow. The port customer tip inquiries were still good. The market formed a stable situation for high-priced white japonica rice, and secondary goods were slightly weak by a few fen. Early thin rice was standing firm, and the prices of yinbian yuan and Yang Du port customers were set. Recently, the appetite for clearing stomachs has been sluggish, due to tight credit and high interest rates, buyers have no intention to trade.

Foreign Imported Xian Rice Suspended Trading Yesterday Afternoon 267

▲ Not Many Transactions in the Morning

Yesterday, the market for foreign imported xian rice was due to the end of the Gregorian year, and many local customers were watching and doing nothing. Furthermore, because the executive committee was elected by the guild yesterday afternoon, the market was closed for half a day, and miscellaneous grains and foreign imported xian rice were all suspended from trading. In the morning, the transactions in the South City were also light, with only 409 bales of sales of Kai Xiang rice, 300 bales of Shashi rice, 200 bales of Siam machine rice, 600 bales of broken rice, and 300 bales of Saigon No. 1. Also, 400 bales of Saigon were ready to be loaded, and the return cargo of Saigon ready to be loaded opened at 4.977 yuan, and the foreign firm sold it for 4.94 yuan, which was all taken by the local hanging order. The selling prices of other rice were similar to the previous market, but people's hearts were in the process of looking good.

North and South Goods: Inexpensive and High-Quality Hunan Lotus Seeds 269

Hunan lotus seeds are a common nourishing food, with a fresh and fragrant aroma, quite different from ordinary ones. Stewing them until soft and adding rock sugar makes for a very pleasant snack. Although this year's production is not particularly abundant, market prices are extremely low, deserving of the reputation for being both inexpensive and of high quality. In the Shanghai market, Guangbang [a merchant group] directly manages production areas, which has long lacked vitality. Currently, top-grade Xiangtan lotus seeds are priced as high as thirty-two yuan. Both those inside and outside the industry are uniformly purchasing them, considering the price is only one-third of the peak price. As for risk, it seems limited. It can be stored for a long time during the winter season without spoiling. In Hankou, the price for high-quality lotus seeds is around twenty-eight yuan, while ordinary ones range from twenty-six to twenty-seven yuan, with slight variations. Few are willing to sell at these prices, and the market's sluggishness is unavoidable. The current prices for various grades in the market are listed below for reference:

Silk and Tea 270

Ping-Shui Gunpowder Tea Shows Slight Improvement in Sales to America

Zhejiang's Ping-Shui green tea has been stagnant in sales for a long time. Recently, with the New Year approaching, European firms are adopting a wait-and-see attitude, making the market situation even more desolate. Yesterday, British firms such as Jardine Matheson, Dent & Co., and the Allied Trading Company purchased over 500 chests of "Xia Mu Ma Zhu" [small, round gunpowder tea] green tea after receiving telegrams from American firms. The market price has dropped by two to three yuan compared to before. There have been no large transactions for "Zhen Mei" [precious eyebrow] or "Zhen Mei" [needle eyebrow] tea. Although there are scattered sales of "Gong Xi" tea from stores and firms, the inventory is quite large, and the market trend is declining. However, there is news that the Russian Assistance Association will start operating next week. It is still difficult to determine the volume of sales.

Mild Trend in Hardware and Pig Lead 271

▲ Market Overview: The pig lead market has been rather quiet recently because factories and merchants who actually use lead are halting purchases due to tight cash flow. However, the supply is not extensive, and inventories are low, so the standard price remains stable. Negotiations for spring sales are underway, but the volume of transactions will likely be less lively than in previous years due to high silver exchange rates.

▲ American Lead: There have not been many transactions recently, but sporadic buying and selling are still active. Yesterday and the day before, the market saw two to three hundred ingots being opened, but no large-scale business has been initiated. The price remains at fifteen yuan and two and a half jiao [cents] per dan [a unit of weight, about 50 kg] (using the Tael scale). The Commercial Press, Hua Feng Type Foundry, foundries, and machinery factories are replenishing their stocks. However, paint companies, litharge factories, and merchants from Tianjin and Hankou show no interest in purchasing.

▲ Hunan Lead: Currently, the arrival of goods is not substantial, and market inventory is low, so prices are favorable. However, due to the sluggishness of American lead, the Hunan lead market has to follow suit with a mild trend. The current market price is estimated at fourteen yuan and eight jiao per dan. Some transactions are occurring among merchants in the Hongkou area, and Ningbo merchants are also showing slight interest, resulting in relatively good small-scale transactions. Several tea merchants are in negotiations for goods to be used in the spring, and it is said that over four hundred dan have already been transacted, with the price at fourteen yuan and six and a half jiao per dan, which is significantly less than in previous years.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

What Should Be Done During the New Year Holiday? 283

— Qiu Lang

Dear children, the New Year is coming soon, and your schools will have a holiday, right? Perhaps you are all preparing beautiful clothes, calling for fresh and sweet candies, and searching for various entertainments to pass this great time? However, I believe that this is not right!

Then what should be done? You must know that precious time is fleeting, and once it is gone, no amount of gold can buy back an inch or a fraction of it! Therefore, during this New Year holiday, you should still study. Although you don't have to go to school during the holiday, you should review all the lessons taught by your teachers throughout the year, as well as writing compositions and practicing calligraphy. If you have any questions, you can bring them up and ask your older siblings. In the morning and evening each day, find suitable exercises to ensure that your studies are not neglected and your bodies become healthier.

The ancients used to say, "Learning and career are like rowing upstream; if you don't advance, you retreat." I hope that younger brothers and sisters will follow this as a guiding principle and strive for continuous improvement in knowledge, making sure that your studies do not regress!

What Kind of Person Was Mr. Cai Songpo? 284

— Dingyi

As soon as December 25th arrives, I remember Mr. Cai Songpo, this martyr.

In the fourth year of the Republic (1915), Yuan Shikai instigated Yang Du and others to establish the Preparatory Society for Peace, sending telegrams to all provinces advocating the imperial system. He also fabricated public opinion and wrote letters of urging. He openly established the Grand Ceremony Preparatory Office, changing the following year to the first year of the Hongxian era. On December 25th of that year, Mr. Cai Songpo, in conjunction with various important figures, sent a telegram from Yunnan to Yuan Shikai, demanding that he abolish the imperial system and abdicate immediately within twenty-four hours. Later, this day was designated as the Yunnan Uprising Memorial Day.

In January of the fifth year of the Republic (1916), although Yuan Shikai still declared the imperial system and changed the era name to Hongxian, seeing that various provinces had successively declared independence and unanimously condemned Yuan, he immediately abolished the imperial system. By May, he died of depression and disappointment. Mr. Cai also, due to excessive labor during the period of resisting Yuan, went to Japan for medical treatment after the event was settled, but his condition deteriorated until November 28th, when the treatment proved ineffective, and Mr. Cai passed away, abandoning the Republic of China, which he had helped to rebuild.

Finally, let me summarize what kind of person Mr. Cai actually was.

He was a model student. Why? Mr. Cai Songpo lost his father at a young age, and his family was very poor, but he was able to encourage himself, study diligently, and comfort his mother. He spent his life in a state of working and studying. In Japan, he went through various struggles and finally completed his studies and returned to China. In this light, isn't he a model student?

He was a model soldier. Why? During his tenure as governor of Yunnan, Mr. Cai Songpo did not disturb the people, did not interfere in politics, was loyal, and handled matters with strictness. He did not accept humiliation, resisted the imperial system, and was willing to sacrifice his life. After the event, he did not take credit. In this light, isn't he a model soldier?

He was a model citizen. Why? Mr. Cai Songpo protected the country and loved the people, risked his life, and only knew justice, not fearing the powerful. In this light, isn't he a model citizen?

Air 285

— Zhen

Air is truly a strange thing. It is invisible and untouchable, so how do we know that there is air in the sky?

Take a short glass and invert it in a basin of water. No matter how deep you push the glass down, the water will not rise to the bottom of the glass. If you tilt the glass, bubbles will be released from the glass, and the water level will gradually rise. From this experiment, it can be proven that air, like other substances, also occupies space. Air floats on the surface of the earth, just like water flows in rivers and seas. However, air is thinner than water, so the existence of air is not as obvious as that of water.

Air is not a simple substance. It contains oxygen, nitrogen, carbon dioxide, water vapor, and five rare gases: argon, helium, neon, krypton, and xenon. These nine gases all have their properties and uses.

Oxygen is heavier than air. It easily combines directly with various metals, like rust, and can support combustion. Its use is to provide people with breathing. Miners and explorers, in the seabed or in mines where there is no oxygen, must bring in oxygen in order not to die.

Nitrogen is lighter than air. It does not combine with various substances and must be at high temperatures and specific temperatures to combine with other substances. Its use is to fill light bulbs because there will inevitably be oxygen present in the light bulbs, so nitrogen is introduced to expel the oxygen. It is also used to manufacture fertilizers.

Carbon dioxide is heavier than air. Water vapor condenses into water when it encounters cold.

The five rare gases: Argon: does not combine with other substances. Some light bulbs contain argon, which are called argon bulbs. Helium: The gas bag in airships is this gas. Neon: Used in nighttime billboards, the various colors are very eye-catching, and this gas is commonly known as neon. Krypton and Xenon: No one has yet invented their uses. Children, study hard now and invent the uses of krypton and xenon in the future!

Making Beautiful New Year's Cards Yourself 286

— Qianheng

Children! The New Year that you have been looking forward to is coming soon. Of course, everyone will inevitably be busy during this New Year – giving New Year's cards. But buying New Year's cards to give away is too uneconomical. Haven't you all learned "Crafts" and "Art" at school?

Here, let's use them to make an inexpensive and beautiful New Year's card!

Materials: 100-pound drawing paper, watercolor paints, pith paper (available in Chinese pharmacies)

Method: First, print the pattern you like or love on pith paper, then color it according to the pattern. Because the color is on pith paper, it is convex, making it look more lively and beautiful. Then cut it out and paste it in the appropriate place on the drawing paper, and then color the drawing paper.

Note: 1. The shape of the drawing paper is not fixed. Rectangular, round, star-shaped, polygonal, etc., are all acceptable. But don't make it too big, because if it is too big, it will look crude. 2. The position of the pasting should also be appropriate and beautiful, leaving a considerable blank space to write names and phrases. But all of these have to be arranged according to your personal intelligence.

New Year's Gifts 288

— Shendinghe

Luo Zhen got up and first wished his grandparents a happy New Year, then wished his father a happy New Year. His father hugged Luo Zhen on his lap.

"Dad, I want your New Year's gift."

His father nodded and said, "Yes," then put Luo Zhen down and walked to his desk, taking out a red paper envelope from the drawer.

"Zhen, this is my New Year's gift for you this year."

Luo Zhen took the red envelope and hurriedly opened it to see. He thought there must be two silver dollars inside, but when he opened it, it was a blank piece of paper with a map of the Republic of China being蚕食 drawn on it, and a few lines of poetry written on it:

"Happy New Year, Happy New Year,

Change into new clothes, wear new hats,

Who has ever remembered the national humiliation firmly.

From this year on, I hope you wake up!

Cast off your past timidity and laziness,

From today on, struggle and strive to run forward."

After reading it, Luo Zhen couldn't help but feel enlightened, and hot tears rolled down. He hugged his father and said, "I'm awake, I'm awake, from now on I will struggle and strive!"

New Method of Making New Year's Cards 289

— Hansheng

The New Year is coming soon! How happy!

When celebrating the New Year, we always have to prepare New Year's cards to send to our friends. I think you will definitely go to the bookstore to buy some very beautiful New Year's cards, and you may not be very happy to make a few yourself and send them to your good friends. In fact, things you make yourself are only better than those you buy, and when your friends receive the homemade New Year's cards you send, they will definitely make some and send them to you. In this way, can't everyone practice handicrafts?

Here I have written down the methods of making several new types of New Year's cards below:

(1) This is an airplane New Year's card. Use cardboard to cut out three pieces, A, B, and C, according to the diagram (the size is determined by yourself according to the proportion); then punch a small hole at point D and use a piece of thread to tie the New Year's greeting card to it. At the black lines, cut with scissors. When sending it to others, you can not have it assembled, let them assemble it themselves after receiving it. It is best if the cardboard is colored; otherwise, paste colored paper on colorless paper, and the color should be simple. The meaning of this New Year's card is "Aviation Saves the Country," and it wishes them (or her) progress as fast as an airplane.

(2) This is a clock-style New Year's card, which means that time is precious and should not be wasted. Cut a shape like a clock according to diagram A. If you want the hands to move, add two tacks. Add a piece of cardboard on the back and glue it to hold, so that the clock can stand.

(3) This is a locomotive New Year's card, which also expresses the meaning of congratulating friends on their progress. Cut out two pieces according to diagram A, and then apply glue according to the instructions in the diagram to combine the two pieces. Paste transparent paper on the windows. Do not apply glue to point E. Make another New Year's greeting card and place it inside, which can be pulled out and read. The colors should be more beautiful as described in the instructions.

(4) This is a plum blossom New Year's card. Plum blossoms are our national flower and bloom in winter. Cut a plum blossom shape according to diagram A and punch a small hole at point F. In addition, cut out five pieces of each item in diagram B, apply color, and then use thread to attach one piece to each hole at point F.

The above are the methods of making four new types of New Year's cards that I have told you. If you children can read my methods and invent many better ones yourselves, that is what I hope most.

Tier 290

— Chonglou

My sister has a daughter named Tier.

I remember when I went to Tianjin to visit my sister, Tier was still in swaddling clothes and couldn't speak yet. Every time I held her in my arms, her two jet-black eyes would always glance at my face. In order to preserve her lively appearance, I had taken several photos of her. Soon after, I left them.

This year, my sister came to Shanghai, and I almost didn't recognize Tier! Because she can now walk, run, and talk. She can also cut paper, cutting out various patterns, including cats, fish, people, utensils, and houses, all of which are very lifelike. I admired that this five-year-old child already had very good art.

I showed her the photos I had taken of her before and said, "This is you." But she shook her little hand and said, "No! No! Look how big I am now."

I sang and danced, and she listened and watched attentively. Soon, she would take two handkerchiefs as wings and learn to "fly like a butterfly."

My sister stayed in Shanghai for a month and then took Tier back to her hometown. Since then, I have not seen her apple-like face and pleasing appearance. Recently, I received a letter from my sister saying, "Tier often calls you 'dancing uncle,' and she hopes you will come home."

Strange Birds 293

— Ganqi

Children, we haven't seen each other for another week. Today, I will tell you some interesting things about birds. I think children will definitely like it!

(1) Birds that are like Tailors

There is a kind of small bird, about the same size as a sparrow. But don't underestimate its short body, its means of building nests are very clever. It draws silk from the silkworms in the wild. Using its beak as a needle, it sews several large leaves together. In this way, its nest is created.

(2) The Crocodile's Toothpick

The ferocious crocodile has a good friend, who is the屑索bird. When the crocodile's enemies come, it makes strange sounds, calling on its friends to escape from them. After the crocodile has eaten its fill, there are always remnants of food stuck in its teeth, which makes it feel very uncomfortable. It opens its mouth wide and waits for the屑索bird to pick out the food. The 屑索bird eats the food to fill its hunger. Children, isn't this very much like the crocodile's toothpick?

Correction Regarding "Famous Continents and Oceans on Earth" 294

— Wen

In the December 2nd issue of this publication, an article entitled "Famous Continents and Oceans on Earth" was written by someone with the pen name Ku. Mr. Ku said that in the past, textbooks divided the world into five continents: Asia, Europe, America, Africa, and Oceania; and five oceans: the Pacific Ocean, the Atlantic Ocean, the Indian Ocean, the Arctic Ocean, and the Antarctic Ocean. He said that this was incorrect and that it should be divided into six continents and four oceans. The six continents are: Asia, Europe, North America, South America, Africa, and Oceania. The four oceans are: the Pacific Ocean, the Atlantic Ocean, the Indian Ocean, and the Arctic Ocean. In fact, what he said is still incorrect.

The correct definition should be seven continents and four oceans.

The seven continents are: Asia, Europe, North America, South America, Africa, Oceania (i.e., the Oceanic continent), and Antarctica.

The four oceans are: the Pacific Ocean, the Atlantic Ocean, the Indian Ocean, and the Arctic Ocean.

The determination of six continents and four oceans also has a considerable history, and it is necessary to describe it here. Now let's look at the explanation below!

The earliest division was indeed five continents and five oceans. However, since 1911, as a result of the exploration of Antarctica by the Norwegian Amundsen et al., it was confirmed that Antarctica was just a landlocked continent covered in solid ice, not an ocean. From then on, it was named Antarctica. In the 22nd year of the Republic (1933), the Ministry of Education also issued an order explaining and confirming the seven continents and four oceans.

This year, in November, U.S. Navy Rear Admiral Byrd's Antarctic expedition used wireless radio to report (see Shen Bao, November 20th and 25th) that Antarctica is not only not an ocean, nor a cluster of islands (as some people claimed), but a vast continent of 20 square miles. Therefore, the addition of Antarctica is certain.

Mr. Science Performs Magic Tricks 296

— Hegongchao

Let's Generate Electricity

Today, Mr. Science brought a kitten and a stick of sealing wax (the sealing wax used to seal the mouths of letters) that was about the length of a cigar onto the stage. It's so cold today. A red-hot electric furnace was placed on the left side of the stage, filling the stage with warmth.

Mr. Science said, "Today we are going to generate electricity. You must think it's strange. Electricity only exists in the sky in summer. How can we generate electricity? But you must know that everything contains electricity. Let's first take this sealing wax stick and try it out."

Mr. Science took out a piece of flannel from his pocket and rubbed it vigorously and quickly on the sealing wax stick. After rubbing it for a while, he immediately called a child to come to the stage and put the heated end of the sealing wax stick to the child's hair. A few strands of hair were attracted up and stuck to the sealing wax stick. After a while, they fell down one by one.

"The sealing wax stick also contains electricity. After I rub it hard, it will heat up, and heating up is a phenomenon of generating electricity. The amount of electricity generated by friction is very small and can only attract extremely light things like hair and paper scraps.

"Let's try this cat again," Mr. Science said, leading the cat to the electric furnace and heating it for a while, so that its body was warm. Then he led it to the center of the stage and rubbed it very quickly on the cat's fur. The cat's fur stood on end and made a very light "creaking" sound. At the same time, Mr. Science asked someone to turn off the lights, and the stage and audience immediately became dark. Then they saw brilliant sparks emitting from the cat's fur.

"This proves that the cat also has electricity in its body. When you want to play these two sets of electric tricks, if you don't have a sealing wax stick, then a fountain pen or an imitation ivory comb can be used. If you don't have flannel, then wool can be used. But when playing, the drier the things you use, the better, and the air must also be dry. It is easy to succeed in playing in this winter. When rubbing, you must use force and be quick.

"To make the cat's fur generate electricity, you can't press the cat's fur tightly, but rub it loosely and quickly, so that electricity can be generated. To see the sparks emitted from the cat's fur, you must play in a dark room."

The tools for the experiment! One cat. One sealing wax stick. One piece of flannel.
