Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Supplement

A Brief Discussion on the Production Techniques of Chinese Films Based on Works Such as "Rebirth Flower" 318

— Ling He

Starting with "Life," it is gratifying to see that Chinese film technology has indeed made significant progress. Of course, the technological progress we demand is definitely not like that of European and American films, which rely on sophisticated technology to exaggerate empty content. What we demand is the complete harmony of content and form.

Generally speaking, capitalist films often have form surpassing content, while emerging films lack new techniques to express new content because appropriate techniques are still being gradually discovered, while capitalist film technology has already developed to its final stage.

However, here I do not want to discuss the entire method of expression, but only want to talk about production techniques, that is, I will not discuss narrative methods or montage, but only sound recording techniques or photography techniques.

In terms of sound films, "Rebirth Flower" must be brought up as an example. Here, Hu Die plays both sisters. When the two sisters appear in the same frame, it is very troublesome in terms of photography. In addition to shooting a scene twice, it is also necessary to use a fake Hu Die's back. This kind of photography method has a considerable effect in satisfying the audience's curiosity, and as a result, it becomes one of the reasons why "Sister Flowers" or "Rebirth Flower" can be a box office success. And the photography technique has improved, for example, the average audience does not notice the traces of the fake. Speaking of sound recording, "Rebirth Flower" has indeed made significant progress compared to previous Chinese sound films. Although the sound effects of the sound film have not been fully utilized, the clarity of the recording, every word, and every song can be understood clearly, which is indeed commendable.

Another example that must be mentioned is "Peach and Plum Calamity". This work certainly has good content and can be called the use of the functions of sound films, but because it was the first attempt at a Three-Friend recording machine, the sound is not clear enough. (Perhaps it was a problem during the printing of the soundtrack.) In terms of photography, except for the re-shot places, it is not clear enough (such as when Yuan Muzhi thought of his wife's painful labor in the factory, re-shooting a person struggling in bed above the furnace, it is impossible to recognize that it is Chen Boer), the rest of the lighting or camera angles are very successful.

In addition, in terms of silent films, I would like to bring up a few for discussion. The excellent photography of "Woman" and "Fragrant Snow Sea" goes without saying, and the recently released films such as "Goddess", "Bigamy", and "Flying Flower Village" all show that the photographers are working very hard. Everyone is deepening their research at an accelerated pace, almost competing extremely on the works. This phenomenon is, in any case, worthy of the joy of people who care about Chinese films.

As for the sets, generally speaking, apart from the fact that they are limited by capital and cannot compete with the so-called magnificent European and American films (in fact, it is not a proper development to work on magnificent sets that are close to waste), in terms of the composition or color of the sets, many films have achieved the level determined by the content, that is to say, the set designers have done their duty to express the content of the works.

As mentioned above, the production technology of Chinese films has indeed made significant progress recently. The previous saying that there is no new form to express new content is now slowly overcoming this difficulty.

Audience Opinions

Review of "Rebirth Flower" 319

— Yafei

After the film "Sister Flowers" broke the stagnant air in the Chinese film scene, it almost became a surprising work that many people valued. However, the reason why "Sister Flowers" was so successful is certainly because the plot can cater to the tastes of ordinary idle petty bourgeois audiences, but the vivid plot, the sorrowful story, the clear photography and sound recording, and the successful performances of Hu Die, Xuan Jinglin, Zheng Xiaoqiu, etc., are all enough to make this film shock the silver screen and break the unprecedented box office record, which is by no means accidental.

Now that I have watched the sequel to "Sister Flowers", "Rebirth Flower", I might as well talk about it casually. Fortunately, commenting on films is originally a matter of benevolence seeing benevolence and wisdom seeing wisdom. Everyone expresses their own opinions.

After Erbao rescued Dabao in "Sister Flowers" out of maternal instinct, it could have ended there, but now to have the extra "Rebirth Flower" seems superfluous. It is written here that after Erbao rescued Dashu from prison, she would encounter many hardships, and the love history between Erbao and a revolutionary youth from the past was forcibly inserted, which is still an expression of the playwright's consistent ending method.

The confusion of the plot and the blandness of the story in this film are really undeniable. For example, writing about Qian Governor, Xiao Regiment Commander, Zhao Da, etc., certainly exposes the ugly behavior of the warlords, but haven't we already seen these in "Sister Flowers"?

There are also some improprieties in the performance, such as: (1) Because Hu Die played two different typical people alone, many of the movements appeared mechanical, especially in several scenes with doubles, and the dialogue could not be consistent, which inevitably dispersed the power of expression. (2) The theatrical atmosphere inside is too strong, making the audience feel like they are watching a civilized play. (3) The incoherent editing is also enough to ruin the success of the play.

However, there are also many things worth noting, such as the appropriate small actions, the clear sound recording, the lively dialogue, the smooth flow, the soft light, and the competence of the actors. The director's handling of the camera angles is also very sophisticated; these can all bring a lot of effects to the performance of the whole play.

Review of "Flying Flower Village" 320

— Zhang Dahui

Whether from the content or form, "Flying Flower Village" and "Spring Tide" have great differences. The former is just a film depicting a love story, while the latter is a realistic work. What the author shows us here is a tragedy caused by economic oppression. A-Hua's wife being seduced by the stationmaster and later becoming a goddess are all explanations that the environment is everywhere subject to economic forces.

The director handles the whole play very lightly and briskly, and the personalities of the characters in the play are clearly portrayed. The photography at the opening describing the scenery of Flying Flower Village allows us to see a poetic picture. In terms of actors, Gao Zhanfei's strong personality, Hu Ping's expression of love for her husband and children, and Chen Juanjuan's innocence and liveliness are all very suitable for the characters in the play. Wang Naidong's villainous role and Qin Tong's portrayal of the old man are also very successful.

As for the final ending, I believe that the stationmaster's punishment and A-Hua's acquittal have fallen into the formula of good and evil retribution. It would be better to end with the stationmaster escaping justice and A-Hua being executed, which would make the whole play more intense and tragic.

My Review of "Rebirth Flower" 321

— Fei Nianzu

Since "Sister Flowers" was released and broke the record for opening dates, it has aroused the attention of the Chinese people to the domestically produced sound films that have always been despised.

Now, "Rebirth Flower", which follows "Sister Flowers", has been released in Xinguang, but after watching the film, I feel that this film is not a very successful work. Although director Zheng Zhengqiu is very hardworking, his greatest shortcoming is that he cannot use the special techniques of sound movies to increase the tragic and joyful elements of the whole play. At the same time, he cannot slightly improve the audience's level, and like "Sister Flowers", he only uses twists and turns to win the audience's tears.

Regarding the actors, Hu Die's Dabao and Erbao still have their special achievements, although there is no progress compared to "Sister Flowers". Xuan Jinglin's old woman is vividly portrayed, showing great progress. Zheng Sheqiu can be regarded as quite diligent. Tan Zhiyuan, Zhu Qiuhen, Wang Xianzai, etc. are also very hardworking. The other supporting roles are also good.

Tianyi Company's new sound film "Renzhu!" Directed by Shao Zuiweng and Gao Lihen—starring Fan Xuepeng, Ye Qiuxin, Chen Qiufeng, and Wei Pengfei—now showing at the Carlton

Secrets of "The Merry Widow" 322

— Yunmen

The songs sung by Jenny MacDonald, the heroine of "The Merry Widow", are "Vilia", arranged by the great musician Le Bo Luoguan; "Tonight Will Teach to Forget" is sung on the balcony; and "Widows Are Gay". The male lead, Heifeler, sings "I am Going Maxims", "Girls! Girls! Girls!", and "The King Can Do No Wrong." The two sing together "Not a Word."

MacDonald leads "Embassy Dance", "The Merry Widow Whirlwind Dance", and the Parisian "Can Can Dance", which was called the irritating springtime in the 19th century.

The violin of the great musician Le Bo Luofu is called unparalleled in the world. Not only is it a thousand-year-old antique, but it can also play dual tones (Bilingual). Generally speaking, no matter how precious a violin is, it can only emit one kind of high tone (Tenor) or low tone (Bass), but Leqin can play both male and female tones. The beauties in Maxim's dance hall in the film are the best choices in Hollywood, a total of fourteen, with five seats in New York Province, and the remaining nine seats belong to other provinces, which shows the meaning of beautiful women being hard to find again.

In "The Merry Widow", there are two new technical attempts. One is the basket weave dance. The dancers on both sides wear colorful clothes, change their heights, and rotate left and right, like butterflies passing through flowers, which is a creation in the history of dance. One is the memory of sound (Muicai Retro pect). The common method of recalling the past on the screen uses dissolving or dissolving into method (Dissove) to make the old images reappear vividly, but in the film, the Count recalls the past, breaking the old method and replacing it with the mood of sound. This is a new technique of using sound instead of color.

"Vortex" Renamed "Femme Fatale" 323

"Vortex" is Yang Xiaochong's proud masterpiece after "Good Night". This drama stars Chen Yanyan and Zhang Yi, with Liang Saizhen as a guest star. Because the roles they play can all be given individual expression, this drama has superior achievements.

Chen Yanyan's performance here is excellent, which goes without saying, and what is most surprising is that Liang Saizhen and Zhang Yi have both made unprecedented gains. According to general opinion, Liang Saizhen seems to have become a new Liang Saizhen in this film, and because Zhang Yi has more opportunities to act here, it has made him the most successful film since joining Lianhua.

"Vortex" will soon meet the public. But the name of "Vortex" seems to need to be changed to a better name. It is rumored that it will be renamed "Femme Fatale".

Film Novel

The Merry Widow (VI) 324

— Su Hua

Speaking to this point, Tang Erna turned around and said to the jurors: "I am guilty. In addition to committing crimes such as treason and dereliction of duty, I have also committed the crime of being fooled. My fate this time can give men a great lesson. When a man can enjoy himself with hundreds of women, if he actually goes to love a woman alone, he is extremely foolish and should be sentenced to death." After he finished speaking, the people in the audience shouted "Tang Erna" with great excitement. The king's attendants immediately rushed to the palace to report the situation of the trial, saying that Tang Erna had confessed his crime. The king heard this and knew that the country was about to go bankrupt. He and the queen were packing their soft luggage and preparing to escape. Just as they were busy, the attendant ran up panting and said, "That...that widow wants to go to the prison to visit Tang Erna." The king and queen heard this and immediately ordered people to go to Bofu and wake up the drowsy Bofu, asking him to invite the prison officials and cabinet members to a meeting. The king said with a happy face, "This plan will not fail."

In the gray prison corridor, Sulia walked step by step. The jailer asked on the side, "Miss, are you a friend of the captain?" "Not much of a friend." "Are you a relative?" "No." "But you knew him before, right?" "Yes." "Then I'm afraid you don't recognize him now. He has completely changed." They talked as they walked, and soon they had reached the door of the cell. The jailer opened the door, and she walked in trembling. There was nothing inside except a bed. At that time, a mouse ran across her instep. The shock scared her to run to the bed. Then Tang Erna walked in. He looked at her as if amused. She said embarrassedly on the bed: "I'm sorry, I was chased in by the mouse." Tang Erna said with a smile, "That mouse chased you from so far away, it's really amazing." Sulia said with a straight face, "Don't think that I came here..." Tang Erna quickly interjected, "To see me? No, definitely not." She replied, "Yes, I came to see you." After she finished speaking, she wanted to leave, but the door was already locked. She pushed hard, and he also came to help push. But there was no result. Hearing no sound outside at all. In fact, at that time, the king was leading a group of people outside listening quietly. Sulia said angrily, "Did you bribe the jailer to lock me in here?" Tang Erna also said, "You must have bribed the jailer to lock yourself in here." Sulia shouted, "I can't stand your insults anymore." "Then why don't you go out?" he asked her. At that time, she really had no way to think. After a while, the small window on the wall opened, and someone sent in fragrant wine and glasses. They looked at each other and had no idea what to do. Tang Erna thought for a while and said, "You didn't bribe the jailer, so he must have locked us together. We were both tricked." Sulia also said, "Then what do we do?" Tang Erna said, "Let's not be intimate." "Yes, let's not be intimate." She also said this. "Let's not fall for his trick. How can we make us fall in love if we hate each other?" She continued. "Okay, let's not fall for his trick." After finishing speaking, Tang Erna went to the small window to get wine to drink. The two drank together. After a while, the intoxicating piano music rang, and the two began to dance. When he wanted to kiss her tightly, she still stubbornly avoided, but when he shouted "A mouse is coming," she rushed to the bed, and he sat beside her with a smile. The eyes of the two communicated with each other, expressing the tacit consent of love. At the same time, the small window opened, revealing the smiling bishop. Before he could finish announcing that he recognized them as a formal couple, Sulia's red lips were already waiting for his passionate kiss. (The End)
